Chapter 952: An Endless Stream of Visitors

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you alright?” Lan Ting came to visit Lu Yang in Sinner Hall with a basket of spirit fruits.

“I’m doing quite well. Thank you for your concern, Junior Sister Lan,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied with a grin. The basket contained several varieties of tasty spirit fruits; it was clear that Lan Ting had put thought into it.

“Why don’t you have some as well?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy offered one to her prison buddy, the Moonchaser True Person, who resided next door.

The Moonchaser True Person didn’t decline, murmuring “thanks” before eating.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy selected a fruit she hadn’t seen before but found appealing and handed it to Lan Ting. “Junior Sister Lan, you have some too.”

The spirit fruits in the basket were divided into three portions by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Eating was an activity that thrived on atmosphere; she wasn’t accustomed to dining alone. Good food was meant to be shared. This reminded her of the gatherings with Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi in the ancient era.

The three of us sat together in harmony.

Lan Ting sized up the Moonchaser True Person with curiosity. “Are you Bai Ye, the one Senior Brother mentioned?”

She's indeed an unfamiliar face. But she knows how to undo the array and enter the medicine repository. Does this suggest that she’s one of the immortal palace’s ancestors?

Lan Ting had asked her shifu about Bai Ye’s identity, but Luo Hongxia had seemed reluctant to elaborate.

The Moonchaser True Person was too embarrassed to reveal her identity, so she could only temporarily borrow Bai Ye’s name. “Yes, I am Bai Ye.”

Inwardly, the Moonchaser True Person apologized to Bai Ye. This is the first lie I’ve ever told in my life.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, could you guide Junior Sister Lan on how to cultivate her immortal physique?” Lu Yang asked, feeling somewhat indebted to Lan Ting for taking care of him at the immortal palace all this time.

“Are you referring to her Genesis Immortal Physique?”

“Yes.”

“Hmm, alright then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was somewhat reluctant, but since it was Lu Yang’s request, she would comply if she could.

“Junior Sister Lan, how is your cultivation of the Genesis Immortal Physique going?”

Lan Ting smiled bitterly. “To be frank, Senior Brother Lu Yang, I’m quite lost. I originally planned to cultivate my golden core, nascent soul, and primordial soul toward pure yin, but they seem to have a mind of their own, constantly absorbing pure yang power and causing the pure yang power within them to become increasingly concentrated.

“I’ve also considered cleansing my primordial soul with pure yin power, but it proved useless.”

The Moon Laurel Immortal Palace’s cultivation techniques leaned toward yin attributes, yet her golden core, nascent soul, and primordial soul insisted on developing toward yang attributes. This compelled her to learn many cultivation and combat methods from other sects, leaving her anxious and uneasy.

She had consulted numerous elders and pored over ancient texts, all to no avail. The Genesis Immortal Physique was rare, and no cultivation methods had been recorded.

In truth, the Moonchaser True Person thought highly of Lan Ting and had secretly searched for cultivation methods for the Genesis Immortal Physique, but it was futile. freewebnovel.com

“Junior Sister Lan, there’s no need to be troubled. This is precisely the cultivation process for the Genesis Immortal Physique,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy instructed earnestly.

“What is ‘genesis?’ Genesis refers to hundun primal chaos, the unity of yin and yang. Although your golden core and primordial soul are of yang attributes, you possess a pure yin body.

“As long as you cultivate step by step until the Fusion Stage, where your primordial soul merges with your body, everything will naturally fall into place. You will achieve your Genesis Immortal Physique with major success then.

“It would be best to have your primordial soul absorb more solar power. That will be beneficial upon reaching the Fusion Stage.”

“Really?” Lan Ting’s eyes sparkled as she listened. The gloom that had long coiled around her heart dissipated.

“This is something I read in an immortal’s handwritten notes.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked inwardly, If you ask where those notes are, this immortal can only write you a copy on the spot.

But how could Lan Ting doubt Lu Yang’s words? She had merely blurted out the question by instinct.

Lan Ting chatted a while longer with “Lu Yang” and the Moonchaser True Person before departing contentedly.

“It seems you and Lan Ting have a good relationship,” the Moonchaser True Person commented with a smile. Though Lu Yang is quite strange and harbors many secrets, he isn’t bad at heart. If there’s an opportunity, I can play matchmaker.

Immediately after, another immortal palace disciple arrived with a fruit basket to visit Lu Yang.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you alright?”

In her original form, Lu Yang would have recognized her, but now that she was in a shrunken state, he struggled to identify who she was.

I think she’s He Miao from the artifact refinement chamber.

“Junior Sister He, I’m fine. Many thanks for your concern, Junior Sister.” With Lu Yang’s tips, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy handled the situation smoothly.

“It’s good that you’re alright, Senior Brother.” He Miao’s cheeks flushed slightly as she looked coyly at “Lu Yang.”

As she was rather bashful, she didn’t dare say much to Lu Yang and soon departed.

“It seems you and He Miao have a good relationship too,” the Moonchaser True Person commented with a smile, though it looked somewhat unnatural.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you alright?”

Yet another immortal palace disciple arrived with a fruit basket to visit Lu Yang.

“Many thanks for your concern, Senior Sister An. This prison is rather peaceful, perfect for cultivating one’s character and mind. It could be considered a fortuitous opportunity.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s responses grew increasingly practiced.

“You and An Qiuxia have a good relationship, too.” The Moonchaser True Person’s smile seemed plastered on, somewhat rigid.

Junior Sister Xia Tang, Junior Sister Huang Shan, Senior Sister Bu Lianxin... “Lu Yang's" room was soon filled with fruit baskets.

Previously, with Lan Ting acting as a barrier, the immortal palace disciples had felt too shy to approach Lu Yang. Now that Lu Yang was in Sinner Hall, everyone could visit him as they pleased, giving them more chances to interact with him.

The Moonchaser True Person. “...”

Did you all read the novels I placed in the scripture library for nothing? Is this Lu Yang kid really so outstanding?!

He just has a better background, higher talent, stronger cultivation, more fortuitous encounters, a better personality, and broader knowledge—aside from that, he’s no different from other cultivators.

“Would you like some more?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed the Moonchaser True Person’s resentful stare and assumed she coveted the fruit baskets.

“I can’t eat any more.”

“Fine then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy resumed eating.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was discerning in her tastes; these spirit fruits didn’t catch her eye. However, she had nothing better to do, and with so many spirit fruits piled here, she couldn’t help nibbling on a few.

Other prisoners cast glances of envy and jealousy toward “Lu Yang.”

Did this kid come to Sinner Hall for a vacation?

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, I have some questions regarding the Sword Dao cultivation. Could you offer some pointers?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered. I have experience dealing with female cultivators, but Sword Dao cultivation isn’t my forte. “Xiao Yangzi, you handle this one.”

True to his reputation as the number one in Sword Dao among peers, Lu Yang’s few words of guidance resolved problems that had plagued Xue Shilou for years. The latter felt that he had seen the light, vaguely glimpsing the path ahead, and joy welled within him.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, will you tell stories again tonight?” Bai Ye asked from behind.

As he was teaching Xue Shilou, day and night had shifted before he knew it. Now, it was Bai Ye in control of the body.

Since Lu Yang is here, I don’t have to go out and play.

“Yes.”

He mused inwardly, Strange. I didn’t seem to be this busy outside. Now that I’m in Sinner Hall, why does it feel like I’m busier than ever?

Chapter 953: Bai Ye Took the Initiative

Sinner Hall, which had always been cold and quiet, had recently become unusually lively. Lan Ting observed this and fretted over it in her heart, but there was nothing she could do.

She had no grounds to stop her senior and junior sisters; after all, there was nothing wrong with visiting a guest.

Though their intentions are hardly pure.

Fortunately, when night fell, the other disciples had a sense of propriety and refrained from disturbing Lu Yang’s rest, allowing Lan Ting to exhale a slight breath of relief.

Though Lu Yang still couldn’t rest at night.

~~~

“Shifu, this is Lu Yang’s current situation,” the shrunken Jinghong said to the jet-black ring in her hand.

She had no idea what her shifu feared and why her shifu dared not probe with spiritual consciousness, leaving her to verbally recount Lu Yang’s situation in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

The consciousness within the ancient black ring pondered a moment, then transmitted an aged and deep voice. “It seems this child’s constitution is somewhat special, innately attracting women. Perhaps what he condensed during the Golden Core Stage was the Harem Golden Core!

“You must keep your distance from him, lest you be influenced by his constitution. Those who can form the Harem Golden Core are often not tolerated by heaven and earth, meeting tragic fates.”

“Understood.”

Jinghong stroked the black ancient ring, feeling immensely reassured.

She had obtained this ring from a secret domain. The existence within the ring was ancient, powerful, and omniscient, guiding her cultivation. Following its instructions, she had gradually improved her constitution, mastered artifact refinement techniques, and advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, achievements that brought her to where she was today.

At the ring’s behest to conceal her abilities, no one in the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace knew the full extent of her skills.

~~~

“Senior Brother’s experiences are truly incredible.” Bai Ye continuously replaced the stories Lu Yang had just told in her mind, lamenting that she couldn’t witness them in person. “What a pity I can’t leave my original form’s territory; otherwise, I can venture into the jianghu with you, Senior Brother.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Bai Ye, if you go down the mountain with your Transcendent Tribulation cultivation, that’s not called ‘venturing into the jianghu’—you’ll be sweeping through the jianghu.

Like the Epoch Immortal, from the moment Bai Ye developed spirit intelligence, she was equivalent to a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“Oh, I could just leave by moving the mountain!” Inspired by Lu Yang’s stories, Bai Ye’s thinking had subtly shifted, growing increasingly clever.

After all, the Great Snow Mountain has so many peaks; moving one wouldn’t matter.

“Wouldn't carrying a mountain around be rather conspicuous?” Lu Yang kindly pointed out the flaw in this idea, though he did feel sorry for Bai Ye and wished he could take her out for a stroll.

The sky-reaching Moon Laurel Tree Ancestor moving a snow-capped mountain—the very thought is terrifying. Anyone witnessing it would take to their heels without a second thought.

A brilliant idea suddenly struck Bai Ye, and she came up with a compromise. “I could move a mountain to your Dao-Seeking Sect instead.”

Although I can’t accompany Senior Brother Lu Yang in venturing into the jianghu, a change of environment would be nice.

Lu Yang opened his mouth, then closed it, realizing he had no reason to refute it.

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded with satisfaction. I knew that Xiao Yangzi and I were of one mind.

“Xiao Yangzi deliberately pointed out how conspicuous moving a mountain would be, thereby subconsciously leading Bai Ye to propose moving the snow mountain to the Dao-Seeking Sect. This level of scheming is already on par with mine.”

“Immortal Fairy, don’t talk nonsense. Bai Ye took the initiative to suggest coming to the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Lu Yang hastily clarified. This makes it seem as though I had hoodwinked Bai Ye into coming to the Dao-Seeking Sect. If Big Senior Sister and Senior Brother Dai misunderstand, the consequences would be dire.

“We’ll definitely say that it was Bai Ye who took the initiative,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied, wearing an expression that said, “this immortal gets it.”

~~~

Early the next morning, the Moonchaser True Person fixed Lu Yang with an unfriendly stare. “Lu Yang, you kid, it’s one thing to have good relations with our immortal palace disciples, but now you want to trick Little Ye into leaving?”

She has only known Lu Yang for a few days, and she already has thoughts of moving a mountain to the Dao-Seeking Sect. If she continues interacting with Lu Yang, who knows what would happen?

“A’Ri, I was the one who took the initiative; it has nothing to do with Senior Brother Lu Yang,” Bai Ye quickly interjected. “Besides, if I go to the Dao-Seeking Sect, can’t you go too?” She couldn’t leave her original form’s territory, and neither could the Moonchaser True Person.

The Moonchaser True Person hesitated for a moment and didn’t counter. Although this may feel like I’ve let down the immortal palace I founded, I do have thoughts of playing somewhere else.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised Lu Yang’s actions effusively. As expected of Xiao Yangzi, he knows that as long as he can hoodwink Bai Ye, Bai Ri will obediently follow her to our Dao-Seeking Sect. If he weren’t already at the pinnacle of officialdom with no further titles to confer on him, I would certainly promote him.

“Xiao Yangzi, how about you become the Dou Emperor now?”

A question mark popped out of Lu Yang’s head. He was puzzled how the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had suddenly conceived such a terrifying idea.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, may I also consult you regarding Sword Dao?” Two cells away, Xuanyuan Tianhen called out. Having witnessed his junior brother Xue Shilou’s great gains from Lu Yang the previous day, he could no longer hold himself back.

“It’s possible, but could you have Fellow Daoist Xue relay your questions?” Lu Yang kindly suggested. With Xue Shilou between them, Xuanyuan Tianhen could only shout, which was too noisy.

“Junior Brother, ask Fellow Daoist Lu Yang: when I execute Falling Goose on Flat Sand Form, I always feel like something is lacking. What exactly is missing?”

Xue Shilou looked at his senior brother with an odd expression. “I can answer that question.”

Xuanyuan Tianhen leaned sideways to stare at Xue Shilou, as if he were meeting him for the first time. “You can answer it? Then why didn’t you say so before?”

“I thought you were deliberately concealing your abilities.”

“Conceal my ass! This is my actual level!” Xuanyuan Tianhen roared in anger.

“Senior Brother, keep your voice down. With that shout, the entire Sinner Hall now knows your Sword Dao level is not up to standard.”

“Conceal my ass! This is my actual level.” Xuanyuan Tianhen repeated in a lower voice, this time audible only to Xue Shilou.

“You don’t need to say it twice; I can hear you clearly,” Xue Shilou said helplessly. He often felt he was the senior brother instead.

“No can do. If I don’t say it twice, I’ll feel stifled inside.” Xuanyuan Tianhen insisted on clear communication and absolutely refused to get the short end of the stick.

“Fine.”

Xue Shilou addressed each of Xuanyuan Tianhen’s questions one by one, though he didn’t know everything. Occasionally, he encountered a difficult problem and had to seek Lu Yang’s help.

“Please excuse the embarrassment,” Xue Shilou said sheepishly.

“Don’t say that. Exchanging insights on Sword Dao benefits not only you and Fellow Daoist Xuanyuan but also greatly aids my improvement.”

Just as Xue Shilou was about to respond, his expression suddenly changed drastically. His face was covered in sweat as he rolled on the ground, howling in pain.

“So noisy,” remarked the Moonchaser True Person from two cells away.

After pondering for a bit, she figured no one would notice and secretly activated her Incipient Dao Fruit, aiming it at Xue Shilou. The latter immediately ceased his cries. Although he was still rolling on the ground, his expression shifted to one of comfort and joy—he was thoroughly enjoying himself.

The Moonchaser True Person’s subtle action eluded everyone, but not the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Making Xue Shilou perceive pain as pleasurable and granting him feelings of joy—could this be the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Chapter 954: Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit

“Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit? Are you saying that one can use the Incipient Dao Fruit to influence emotions?” Lu Yang watched as Xue Shilou writhed on the ground like a maggot in the adjacent cell, the latter displaying an expression of blissful enjoyment.

A peculiar expression crossed Lu Yang’s visage.

I wonder what expression Xue Shilou would wear upon waking up. Probably, he may not want to live anymore?

“Since one cannot endure pain, one might as well accept it and even revel in it.”

“Fellow Daoist Xue has comprehended such a mental state even while mired in this predicament. He’s truly impressive.”

“A role model for us all!”

Observing Xue Shilou’s behavior, the other inmates felt that his mental state was extraordinary and that he would surely achieve great things in the future.

“Yes, the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit can make people happy, angry, scared, and so on. In ancient times, several people condensed this Incipient Dao Fruit. I recall one called the Bliss Supreme Lord, who was the most active; he could freely change others’ emotions.

“For example, if he hit someone, that person wouldn’t be angry at all and would even be overjoyed.

“For example, he could make anyone fall in love with him, regardless of gender.

“For example, he could eliminate his own fear, allowing him to face any danger or peril with composure.

“For example, he could plunge his opponents into sorrow, rendering them not in the mood to fight. Alternatively, he could plunge them into rage, clouding their judgment.

“In any case, there were many applications.”

“What happened to him later?”

“Later, he fought the Nine-Layers Immortal. Back then, both were half-immortals and roughly at the same level, so it was difficult to determine a victor.

“Thus, the Bliss Supreme Lord plunged the Nine-Layers Immortal into sorrow, trapped in it.

“As you know, sorrow is often linked to anger. After being consumed by sorrow, the Nine-Layers Immortal quickly grew enraged, his veins bulging and his eyes bloodshot. In that burst of emotions, he let out a couple of roars. His strength surged, and he eliminated the Bliss Supreme Lord.

Oh, by the way, that person with the Harem Golden Core also had the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit. According to him, he comprehended ‘love’ from his harem, and from there, he comprehended the ‘Seven Emotions.’

”Ever since obtaining the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit, even more female cultivators liked him.

“You know his fate, too. The female cultivators loved him so much that they couldn’t bear to part with him, so they parted his corpse, each taking a piece for themselves.

“I had witnessed it from afar back then. All the female cultivators clutched parts of his body, their faces and clothes covered in blood. They even wore eerie, maniacal smiles. It was rather terrifying.”

Lu Yang shuddered. That kind of scene is indeed horrifying. Fortunately, I won’t ever encounter something like that.

As he mused, he casually picked a spirit fruit from a basket and began eating. “The taste is not bad. I’ll buy ten jin later for Big Senior Sister to try.” He was eating an unfamiliar white spirit fruit, and it was surprisingly delicious.

“You call this not bad? Wait until I breed a new variety of Everlasting Immortal Fruit for you to try. Now that will be truly delicious.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned her nose up at Lu Yang’s lack of discernment.

“If my memory serves me right...wasn’t the function of the Everlasting Immortal Fruit to prevent corpses from decaying?” Lu Yang always had the feeling that the Everlasting Immortal Fruit was meant for the dead.

“The function is the function, and the taste is the taste—they’re too different things.” The Everlasting Immortal Fruit was meticulously grown by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself. Setting aside its functions, its taste was naturally top-tier.

“Just follow this immortal and enjoy a peaceful life of comfort. Back in the ancient era, only immortals and a few individuals like Little Ling and the others could eat this.”

Lu Yang didn’t reply, mainly because he wasn’t sure whether he was enjoying a peaceful life of comfort or a peaceful life of suffering.[1]

Seeing that no one had noticed her, the Moonchaser True Person resumed her cultivation with a clear conscience.

To elevate the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit’s state, the most crucial thing was to observe the myriad facets of life and comprehend worldly emotions.

Sinner Hall is filled with anger, sorrow, fear, and hatred—perfect for cultivation.

Of course, there is also joy.

The Moonchaser True Person opened her right eye and glanced at Lu Yang to her right. That’s where the joy is.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you alright?”

Hearing yet another visitor, Lu Yang turned, plastering on a professional smile. “I’m fi...Junior Sister Tao?!”

Lu Yang looked as if he had seen a ghost. Why is Junior Sister Tao here?

“It’s me.” Tao Yaoye smiled sweetly, carrying a cloth bundle. “I haven’t seen you in a long time, Senior Brother. You’ve grown so small.” Tao Yaoye crouched down, speaking to Lu Yang through the bars. Her joy seemed to transmit right through them.

“Junior Sister, what brings you to the immortal palace?” Lu Yang managed a strained smile. He was afraid Tao Yaoye would spread news of his diminution upon returning.

Although everyone in Sinner Hall knows I’ve shrunk, they can’t leave anytime soon, so there’s no rush there.

But Junior Sister Tao is different; who knows if she would capture this in a Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?

“I heard you were visiting the immortal palace, Senior Brother. I’ve longed to see it myself, so I seized this opportunity to come and look around. I just didn’t expect you to have a little accident.” Tao Yaoye looked at Lu Yang, struggling to suppress the urge to pat his small head.

Seeing through Lu Yang’s concern, Tao Yaoye declared, “But don’t worry, Senior Brother, I won’t tell anyone that you’ve shrunk.”

“Thank you, Junior Sister.” Lu Yang breathed a sigh of relief. Junior Sister Tao is reliable after all.

The Moonchaser True Person covertly observed fluctuations in Lu Yang’s emotions. “Quite a series of ups and downs.”

“Senior Brother, why do you have so many fruit baskets? Can you finish them all?” Tao Yaoye looked in surprise at the fruit baskets all over the floor.

Lu Yang smiled wryly. How could I possibly finish them all?

“If you can’t finish them, Senior Brother, they’re just taking up space here. Why not let me take some back as gifts for the other senior and junior brothers when I return to the sect?”

“I’ll have to trouble you then, Junior Sister.”

Tao Yaoye beamed as she took one fruit basket after another. “Your matters are my matters, Senior Brother. It’s no trouble at all.”

She opened her cloth bundle to reveal a four-tier lunch box. “By the way, Senior Brother, I’ve been practicing culinary skills recently and made a bit extra on the side. I don’t know if it will suit your taste, but if you don’t mind, you could try it.”

“Anything Junior Sister Tao cooks must be heavenly.” Lu Yang smiled, thinking to himself that he could finally stop snacking on spirit fruits and pretending they were seeds.

After chatting for a while, Tao Yaoye took her leave. “I still have some matters to attend to, so I’ll make a move first. I will visit you again tomorrow, Senior Brother.”

“Take care, Junior Sister.” Lu Yang waved goodbye.

Even Lu Yang failed to notice the recording orb hidden in Tao Yaoye’s sleeve, which had captured his childlike appearance.

Tao Yaoye’s cooking was indeed excellent; even a Divine Transfiguration-level spirit chef couldn’t do better. The dishes were exquisitely arranged and matched each other, all prepared with rare ingredients highly beneficial for cultivation.

As Lu Yang ate, he ruminated over a question.

“I’ve been at the immortal palace for several days now. Why did Junior Sister Tao only just arrive? Does it take this long to travel from the Dao-Seeking Sect to the immortal palace?

“Or did she just hear about it from Man Gu?”

~~~

Tao Yaoye walked out of Sinner Hall, raising her right hand to shield her eyes from the glaring sun as she looked toward the figure waiting for her at the entrance.

“Junior Sister Lan, I totally never expected you to take the initiative to contact me and inform me of Senior Brother Lu’s situation.”

1. These two sound really similar in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 955: Joining Hands Against Common Foes

Man Gu had informed only Dai Bufan about Lu Yang’s visit to the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

Tao Yaoye had received an urgent message sent over a thousand li from Lan Ting, which was why she had rushed to the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

Getting to see such a tiny Senior Brother Lu Yang already made this trip worthwhile.

Lan Ting snorted coldly. “It’s merely because I was short-handed.” With Lu Yang imprisoned in Sinner Hall, an endless stream of immortal palace disciples came to visit him. Unable to stem the tide as a lone branch, Lan Ting had no choice but to enlist Tao Yaoye’s help.

“I never expected even you to become so small, Junior Sister Lan.” As an adult, Tao Yaoye possessed a natural sense of superiority and didn’t bother quarreling with a little tyke like Lan Ting.

Lan Ting replied unhurriedly, “Being small has its advantages. For instance, Senior Brother Lu and I get to be like close childhood friends. This is surely an experience you will never have, Junior Sister Tao.”

The two stared intently at each other, attempting to find a flaw in the other party’s expression.

Unfortunately, it was futile.

“Never mind. Why should I bother being angry with a little tyke like you? Tell me about the current situation.

Lan Ting’s brow was furrowed. “It’s not looking optimistic. I don’t know how many in the immortal palace harbor designs on Senior Brother Lu Yang, but plenty came yesterday under the pretext of visiting. And since they got their way this time, once Senior Brother Lu Yang is released, they will still have excuses to visit him.”

“This is indeed troublesome.” There’s already Lan Ting competing with me for Senior Brother Lu Yang. If potential rivals from the immortal palace are allowed to interact with him and become real rivals, the competition would become even more arduous.

“It seems the priority now is to prevent them from entering Sinner Hall to visit Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

“Why don’t we just say that Senior Brother Lu Yang is in seclusion and shouldn’t be disturbed?”

“That won’t work. Once Senior Brother Lu Yang is out, a simple question would expose the lie. Moreover, if others can’t enter Sinner Hall for this reason, neither can we.”

This rare opportunity to interact with Lu Yang in such a special place as Sinner Hall was precious. Visiting him could improve his impression of them, and future conversations with him would revolve around topics unique to their shared experiences. After chatting, they could even exchange a smile. Hence, neither of them would easily give up this chance.

We must devise a method that gets the best of both worlds.

“Senior Sister Lan Ting, what are you doing standing here? And who is this...” A voice interrupted their thoughts.

Lan Ting turned to see He Miao from the artifact refinement chamber. “Ah, Junior Sister He Miao, are you here to visit Senior Brother Lu Yang again? Let me introduce her to you. This is Tao Yaoye from the Dao-Seeking Sect. The currently trending Dreamlike Bubble Mirages are her creation.”

Tao Yaoye raised a hand to stop Lan Ting’s introduction. “The Dreamlike Bubble Mirage isn’t solely my achievement. Senior Brother Lu Yang assisted me tremendously and put in considerable effort. He even coined the name ‘Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.’”

“Greetings, Senior Sister Tao.” He Miao hadn’t expected her to be the renowned Tao Yaoye. And from the sound of it, her relationship with Senior Brother Lu Yang is far from ordinary.

“I’m not here for other reasons. I heard that Senior Brother Lu Yang has entered your Sinner Hall and came to visit him.” Tao Yaoye sighed. “I just visited Senior Brother Lu Yang and found his place littered with fruit baskets. He barely has room for his feet. With so many spirit fruits, how could he possibly finish them alone?

“Moreover, Senior Brother Lu Yang has been constantly receiving your immortal palace’s senior and junior sisters during the day, leaving him exhausted physically and mentally. Imprisoned to his right is a criminal afflicted with some unknown ailment, constantly writhing on the ground and chuckling eerily. I suspect he didn’t rest well last night; when I saw him this morning, he seemed utterly listless.”

After He Miao, more immortal palace disciples arrived one after another: An Qiuxia, Xia Tang, Huang Shan, Bu Lianxin...

Seeing that no one was entering Sinner Hall and that Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting were engaged in what seemed to be a serious conversation at the entrance, they felt too embarrassed to pass between them and go inside.

“Who is she?”

“She is Tao Yaoye, the inventor of Dreamlike Mirage Bubbles and also Senior Brother Lu Yang’s fellow disciple. She’s here to visit him.”

“She is Tao Yaoye?”

Having invented Dreamlike Bubble Mirages brought an unceasing stream of spirit stones flowing into Tao Yaoye’s pockets. Her wealth far surpassed that of her peers, and only a few at the Fusion Stage could compare.

After learning of Tao Yaoye’s identity as the inventor and hearing of her special connection with Lu Yang, the immortal palace disciples naturally felt somewhat inferior in her presence.

“I saw that Senior Brother is honestly having a rough time in Sinner Hall. I plan to speak with Palace Leader Luo about temporarily suspending visits to him. That would save everyone the trouble.”

“No!” Lan Ting hastily interjected, echoing the sentiments of the immortal palace disciples.

If visits to Lu Yang are outright banned, wouldn’t we have no more reason to interact with him?

Tao Yaoye observed Lan Ting with keen interest. “Junior Sister Lan, may I ask what identity you are using to stop me? Is it because you have the closest relationship with him in the entire immortal palace? Or is it because you completed a mission together, risking your life to defeat an Everlasting Creed branch leader with him?”

Lan Ting sighed. “I have no identity worth mentioning. However, Senior Brother is a guest I invited after all. Should any issue arise, I ought to bear the responsibility.

“Yesterday, our senior and junior sisters kept visiting Senior Brother Lu Yang, disturbing his rest, yet I failed to stop them. That was our immortal palace’s fault. Thus, I hope we can rectify this mistake promptly.

“Junior Sister Tao, since you feel there were too many visitors yesterday, how about we reduce the number of visits from today onward? Please supervise me.”

Tao Yaoye stared at Lan Ting for a while, deliberating whether to trust her. Finally, she sighed and relented. “Very well, I’ll trust you this once.”

Seeing that Tao Yaoye wouldn’t complain to the palace leader, Lan Ting and the immortal palace disciples exhaled in relief.

Lan Ting stood on a large rock, waving her tiny hand to attract everyone’s attention. “Dear senior and junior sisters, you’ve all surely heard the agreement between Junior Sister Tao and me just now.”

Everyone acknowledged Lan Ting’s identity—she had invited Lu Yang, shared a life-and-death bond with him, and had prevented Tao Yaoye from seeking out the palace leader. She could represent them in making agreements with Tao Yaoye.

Lan Ting continued, “Senior Brother Lu Yang is already aware of our immortal palace’s hospitality and etiquette. However, the continuous visits have indeed inconvenienced him. I take primary responsibility for this.

“To ensure Senior Brother Lu Yang rests well, I believe the best approach is for all of you to prepare meals, and I will bring these meals to visit him, representing everyone.

“I will inform Senior Brother Lu Yang, who prepared each meal I bring, so that he knows of everyone’s kind intentions.”

The crowd murmured among themselves. If they could have Lu Yang taste their cooking and leave a deep impression, that would be an acceptable compromise.

Tao Yaoye frowned. She stepped forward and said, “Senior Brother Lu Yang’s appetite is limited. He wouldn’t be able to eat that much food. Three meals a day will suffice.”

“Then how do we select who prepares the meals? Drawing lots?”

Lan Ting hurriedly said, “Our purpose in visiting Senior Brother Lu Yang is to ensure he rests well and eats well. Therefore, why not base it on culinary skills? Those who cook best may visit Senior Brother Lu Yang and deliver meals to him.”

Lan Ting grasped Tao Yaoye’s intent. With a culinary contest, the others won’t compete with me for the right to visit Senior Brother Lu Yang. Instead, they will turn to internal rivalry, vying over whose cooking is most delicious and whose meals will leave the deepest impression on him.

Chapter 956: Out of Control

Lu Yang noticed that these past few days had been more peaceful. Only Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting brought him meals; no one else came to visit.

This is what normal prison life should be like. The previous endless stream of visitors is certainly abnormal.

Though whether it is normal or not has little to do with me; after all, it is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy serving the sentence.

During the day, the Moonchaser True Person kept secretly observing Lu Yang. She couldn’t help but feel that Lu Yang was perpetually in a foolishly happy state. Such pure joy was something she had never encountered before. Even if she used her Incipient Dao Fruit to maintain a state of joy, she couldn’t achieve such purity.

“Could this be the legendary childlike innocent heart?”

The childlike innocent heart was a state all cultivators pursued, but as far as the Moonchaser True Person knew, no one had ever attained it.

“Peculiar kid.”

“Hmm? My cultivation is returning?” Lu Yang sensed his cultivation gradually increasing—Qi Training, Foundation Establishment...all the way up to the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“It looks like you will soon return to your original size,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked with some regret. Xiao Yangzi has to grow up eventually.

Sure enough, half a day later, white smoke emanated from Lu Yang, obscuring his view. Seizing the opportunity, he quickly retrieved suitable clothing from his identity jade tablet and finally restored his original appearance.

“Whew, moving around in my original form is much more convenient.” Lu Yang hopped a couple of times on the spot, cherishing his current state immensely.

Setting aside everything else, I can at least lift a spirit fruit with one hand, unlike when I was a child and had to hug it with both hands.

“Since I’ve returned to normal, that means the senior and junior sisters of the immortal palace have changed back, too.

“Fellow Daoist Xue, I’ll be taking my leave then.” Lu Yang cupped his hands in goodbye to Xue Shilou.

Five days had passed; he could now leave Sinner Hall.

The Moonchaser True Person watched Lu Yang’s figure until he vanished, lost in thought.

To perfect the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit, the most pivotal thing was to observe the myriad facets of life. These past few days observing Lu Yang had been extremely fruitful for her understanding of joy.

She covertly summoned her Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit. It resembled seven building blocks pieced together, gradually showing signs of solidifying.

“Pure joy... Strange. Why do I feel that aside from joy, this kid Lu Yang also likes himself?”

The Moonchaser True Person knitted her brows slightly, unable to make sense of Lu Yang’s state.

“Is it narcissism? It doesn’t seem like it.

“Pure joy... liking oneself...”

Images of her observations of Lu Yang from the past few days continuously surfaced in her mind. The more she recalled, the harder it was for her to figure it out.

In her palm, the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit trembled incessantly, as if on the verge of coming apart.

The Moonchaser True Person’s expression shifted drastically. “Oh crap...”

~~~

“Elder Mo Ran, this junior shall take his leave now.” Lu Yang bid goodbye to Elder Mo Ran and officially left Sinner Hall.

Elder Mo Ran was rather reluctant to see Lu Yang go. When this kid was around, the interior and exterior of Sinner Hall had been much livelier, providing ample inspiration for my writing.

“Finally out.” Lu Yang stretched his neck. Free from Sinner Hall’s array suppression, his restored power could now be used freely.

“I'll go find Junior Sister Tao first.”

I’m staying in the first guest room; Junior Sister Tao should be next door.

Sinner Hall was far from the guest rooms. Without a special reason, flying was prohibited within the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. Lu Yang had no choice but to walk back.

“By the way, Xiao Yangzi, you may encounter a small problem later,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly warned.

“A small problem?” Lu Yang was puzzled. This is the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace; what problem could there be?

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you’re out!” A somewhat familiar voice sounded.

Lu Yang turned to see He Miao, who had visited him before.

“So it’s Junior Sister He Miao. Many thanks for your concern. It seems you’ve also returned to normal. That’s truly a cause for celebration...”

Before Lu Yang could finish, He Miao threw herself into his arms, gazing at him with limpid eyes.

“Junior Sister He Miao, have you encountered some danger?” Lu Yang was at a loss, bewildered by her actions.

“Senior Brother, I like you!”

“Ah?” Lu Yang grew even more at a loss.

“Senior Brother, how about the two of us go down the mountain together to wander the world, explore the wonders of the mundane realm?”

“Wait, wait, wait, wait, Junior Sister He Miao, please calm down first.” Lu Yang steadied He Miao by the shoulders. He couldn’t help but feel that something was amiss. “Isn’t this rather impulsive? We can sit down and talk slowly...”

“Senior Brother, do you like someone else?”

Lu Yang’s head was filled with question marks.

“Senior Brother, you can only like me!” A jade vase flew forth from behind He Miao, its mouth emitting a gentle beam of light.

Lu Yang’s hair stood on end. He had heard Lan Ting mention this light beam before. Though it appeared gentle, it possessed the effects of an Immobilization Technique. I absolutely mustn’t be caught in it!

Lu Yang shifted his foot and leaped backward, narrowly evading the vase’s attack, then turned and took to his heels.

“Senior Brother, you can’t escape!” A leaf appeared beneath He Miao’s feet. It enlarged, resembling a small boat that could glide over snow.

Whether I can escape or not, I’ll worry about that later; I’ll run first.

He Miao’s cultivation couldn’t compare to Lu Yang’s. Even when piloting her flying leaf, her speed was much slower, allowing Lu Yang to let out a slight sigh of relief.

Suddenly, another figure happened to pass by, staring in astonishment at Lu Yang as he sped toward her.

“Junior Sister An Qiuxia, quickly go check on Junior Sister He Miao! I’m not sure what happened to her...”

“Never mind Junior Sister He! Senior Brother, you’re mine!” An Qiuxia summoned a golden page. It glowed brightly, and countless characters flew out, morphing into ropes that shot toward Lu Yang.

Lu Yang dared not touch these ropes. He hurriedly dodged and fled once more.

“Why are you running? Stop there!” An Qiuxia cried out coquettishly. She stepped onto the golden page and flew after Lu Yang.

With An Qiuxia ahead and He Miao behind, Lu Yang had no choice but to escape to the left.

Immediately after, Junior Sister Xia Tang appeared, blocking his path. Behind her came Junior Sister Qing Feng, Senior Sister Ming Jing, Senior Sister Luo Luo... Each displayed their abilities, intent on capturing Lu Yang.

“What’s going on?!” Lu Yang suddenly recalled the “small problem” that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned.

This problem doesn’t look small at all!

“That lass Bai Ri’s cultivation isn’t up to par; her Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit has gone out of control. As for its effect, judging by this, it probably makes all cultivators within the immortal palace like you?

“The Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit even tried to control me, but my cultivation is too profound; a mere Incipient Dao Fruit can’t affect me. However, these people can’t resist it.”

“Then shouldn’t we go find Senior Moonchaser now and have her stop using her Incipient Dao Fruit?”

“When the Incipient Dao Fruit goes out of control, it’s not something that little lass Bai Ri can handle. But it’s not a big problem. When night falls, and Bai Ye appears, the use of the Seven Emotions Incipient Dao Fruit will naturally cease.”

Lu Yang looked back at the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace disciples, who seemed intent on tearing him limb from limb. Despair welled up in his heart.

“But it’s only early morning now!”

~~~

Chapter 980: Chapter 979: Invitation

Chapter 980 -979: Invitation

The youth sprinted frantically through the torrential rain, with several corpses haphazardly strewn behind him, their blood blending with the rainwater and staining the ground red.

He pushed open the wooden door and, seeing his little sister unharmed, didn’t care how muddy the ground was and sat down at the doorway, bursting into laughter.

As he laughed, he started to cry, then stood up and hugged his little sister tightly, as if she were a cherished treasure regained, unwilling to let go.

“Little sister, you’re finally safe,” he said.

The little sister, overwhelmed by the teenager’s actions, wanted to say something but didn’t know what to say, so she just gently patted his back.

Just as she tried to say some comforting words, she found that the teenager had already fallen asleep on her shoulder.

The youth had a very long dream.

In his dream, he saw his sister die before his eyes, and then the murderer killed him as well.

But he didn’t actually die; instead, he returned to the day before the incident with his sister.

Thinking it was just a dream, he didn’t think much about it, but when he realized the dream was turning into reality, he panicked. Everything was just as it had been the first time, with his sister dying before his eyes.

When he returned to the day before once again, he was eager to tell his sister everything he had experienced, but just as he was about to speak, everything faded to black, a relentless darkness engulfing him, and he returned to the starting point again.

He mustn’t speak of the strange occurrences happening to him, a revelation he had somehow received.

To save his sister, he went through many reincarnations, relying on the knowledge he gained with each cycle to secretly manipulate events. Finally, on the seventh reincarnation, he defeated the murderer, and his sister survived.

He opened his eyes, lying on the bed. His muddy clothes had been removed by his sister, and she had also wiped his body clean. From another room came the sound of water, probably his sister washing his clothes.

The youth had never felt the bed to be such a warm place.

He lifted his right hand, scrutinizing his fingers as if he were examining the ceiling, remembering the seven reincarnations as if they were a dream.

The youth muttered to himself, his eyes showing a hint of confusion: “What on earth is going on?”

Even in the storybooks about cultivators, there was nothing like this.

...

The seven reincarnations were not the endpoint of the reincarnation event, but the starting point.

Since then, Lu Yang had encountered hundreds of reincarnations, both big and small.

This made Lu Yang feel more and more that it wasn’t just the Time Dao Fruit user playing around, nor was it a battle.

Lu Yang’s side had also never found any information about the Time Dao Fruit user.

According to Eldest Senior Sister, Jiang Pingan had used the Power of National Fate to observe the entire Great Xia in several reincarnations, trying to find something different from the previous cycles, but he hadn’t found any useful clues.

Lu Yang had gone to the Fairy Palace to see the Yingtian Immortal, who also had no idea, only saying that probably the opportunity hadn’t come yet, and if destined, they would eventually meet.

Lu Yang translated Yingtian Immortal’s words for himself: I don’t know how to find the Time Dao Fruit user either.

At the peak of Sky Gate Mountain, Lu Yang sheathed his Sword Qi, signaling the end of this training session.

Every time he trained, Lu Yang was on tenterhooks, afraid of encountering a time reversal and losing his progress for nothing.

Thanks to that unseen user, Lu Yang had already let six hundred hours of training results go to waste.

“Just consider it as refining my state of mind,” Lu Yang consoled himself.

“Second-in-command, you have a letter,” Mengmeng waved a tan envelope as she ran over.

“My letter?”

Lu Yang had received many letters, being famous not only for his high cultivation level and rich experience but also for his gentle nature. Many cultivators and mortals had written to him, some wanting to meet him, some requesting his autograph, some wishing to share insights, and even some sending outright confessions.

Lu Yang thought it was another admirer’s letter, but upon opening it, he realized it was not.

“From Kaihuang Temple in Buddha Country?”

Lu Yang had no recollection of Kaihuang Temple, but after reading the letter, he suddenly realized.

“So they’re inviting me to make a show of support.”

“Make a show of support?” Yun Mengmeng was puzzled.

“In the letter, Kaihuang Temple mentioned that Master Shi Chan had discussed me during a sermon there. Coincidentally, they’re holding the Buddha Bathing Festival and there’s also a competition among cultivators. They hope I can grace them with my presence as a judge.”

“Buddha Country practices a theocratic governance system, meaning that Kaihuang Temple is not just a temple but also manages the local city, much like our government offices.”

“However, Kaihuang Temple is not a major temple and doesn’t manage a significant city. Their asking me to come and lend my influence to make a good impression is very likely.”

If it were a major city or a major temple, Lu Yang would certainly have some recollection of it.

“I see.”

Although Yun Mengmeng didn’t quite understand, she nodded anyway.

“So, are you going?”

Lu Yang put away the envelope, “Kaihuang Temple doesn’t seem to have any ulterior motives, and since I’ve never been to Buddha Country, it would be good to visit.”

Considering the reputation of his master and the second senior brother in Buddha Country, Lu Yang generally hesitated to go there, to avoid any man-made difficulties.

This time, being invited as a notable guest was a rare opportunity, so of course, he intended to go.

“Sister Mengmeng, do you want to go?”

“Is there anything tasty in Buddha Country?” Yun Mengmeng was most concerned about this.

Lu Yang recalled the specialities of Buddha Country, “Due to religious beliefs, there is basically no meat in Buddha Country, only vegetarian food, which is exceptional.”

“Then never mind.” Yun Mengmeng’s interest in Buddha Country drastically reduced, “Just bring me some specialities from Buddha Country when you come back, Second-in-command.”

“Agreed.”

Immortal Fairy emerged, her face showing confusion as she recalled the traditions of Buddhism, “It’s rather strange, when we five were creating Buddhism, I always advocated not to distinguish between vegetarian and non-vegetarian food. Yingtian Immortal and the other four insisted that Buddhism should avoid meat and consume more vegetarian food, even saying that since I was the founder of Buddhism, I should follow the rules and make more vegetarian food later on. All four of them said this, so I had to agree to the dietary restrictions of Buddhism.”

Kaihuang Temple wasn’t sure the envelope would reach the Seek Dao Sect, so they sent it many days in advance. There’s still some time until the Buddha Bathing Festival, so Lu Yang could prepare slowly.

Chapter 981 -980: Learned the Principle

“Eldest Senior Sister, Junior Brother Meng and I would like to go to Buddha Country,” Lu Yang, always honest, reported his plans before leaving.

She always said that the junior brother was different from their master, having an excellent reputation outside, and was a very outstanding cultivator.

Those who could stand against Ye Zijin were at least of the Body Integration Realm, no limit in number; even if Lu Yang was confident in his own cultivation level, he had no confidence in dealing with so many people and using Old Meng as bait in a critical moment would probably be futile.

As soon as they set foot in the Buddha Country, a fierce wind whipped up the sand, forcing them to maintain a layer of spiritual essence as a protective barrier just to move normally.

Although the sand blasting their faces wasn’t harmful, it was still quite uncomfortable.

“Buddha Country has been established for three hundred thousand years; haven’t they thought about planting trees?” Meng Jingzhou, annoyed by the sand, took a deep breath and blew out forcefully, fighting against the wind, clearing the sand in front of them.

A Spirit Transformation Great Power had an extraordinary lung capacity. Lu Yang guessed Old Meng could keep blowing like this for a quarter of an hour.

Unlike the frequently changing dynasties of the Central Continent, Buddha Country, situated on the Western Continent, was essentially founded at the same time as the Great Qian Dynasty, boasting a history of three hundred thousand years.

Buddha Country, established on the foundation of Buddhist faith, had a rather loose structure, unlike Great Xia where decrees were enforced uniformly across all cities; there was strong independence among the cities.

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, “Plant trees? The area of Buddha Country is as vast as Great Xia, covered in sand everywhere. Even if you had Pass Tribulation cultivators running around for a lifetime, they couldn’t cover it all with trees. Even an order from the Western Temple wouldn’t be effective.”

The Western Temple, with its long history, was the largest temple and also the ruler of Buddha Country. For example, the official documents the Seek Dao Sect often received, requesting the return of Ye Zijin, were issued by the Western Temple.

“When the Four Ancient Immortals were shaping the continents, they probably pooled all the deserts from the stars here, along with those uninhabitable stars, bare and sterile, thus forming what is now the Buddha Country. It’s already remarkable that it’s inhabitable.”

The camels, terrified by the bloodthirsty aura of the Sand Wolves, trembled. Some ran away with their loads, while others simply lay on the ground.

The merchants, well-versed in the ways of the world, each drew their curved blades in a desperate fight for survival. The Sand Wolves were ferocious, but the merchants were no match for these bloodthirsty creatures.

Sand Wolves were the last thing merchants wanted to encounter on their journeys, more often deadly than not, with only a slim chance of survival.

Suddenly, one Sand Wolf took advantage of a merchant’s distraction and pounced fiercely, tackling Old An to the ground.

Old An fiercely resisted the Sand Wolf’s claws with his curved knife, but the Sand Wolf was incredibly strong, and Old An quickly started to lose the struggle for control.

“Old An!”

Just as they fell into despair, a stern voice broke through like a thunderclap.

“Wicked beast, cease your arrogance!”

In the midst of the swirling sands, a figure soared in the sky, seeming like Buddha Himself, with His two fingers joined together and a halo that symbolized the Consummation of Buddhist practice at His back.

The halo suddenly dispersed, turning into countless Sword Qi, piercing precisely through the skulls of the Sand Wolves.

Another divine figure formed a Fist Seal with his hands, and the golden Swastika Fist Seal exploded forth, shattering the brains of the Sand Wolves.

Old An pushed the lifeless Sand Wolf off and quickly knelt to kowtow. “Thank you, Master, for your grace in saving our lives.”

The others also came to their senses and knelt to express their gratitude to the two divine figures.

Lu Yang landed, smiling slightly. “Benefactors... there is no need for such formalities. My Junior Brother and I just happened to pass by and it was merely a matter of convenience. Please, rise.”

At that moment, Meng Jingzhou also came over, shooting Lu Yang a glance: Your idea of a ‘matter of convenience’ is to extravagantly deploy countless Sword Qi?

Lu Yang returned Meng Jingzhou a look: Are you any better, using Arhat Fist against a group of Demon Beasts that have just entered the Qi Cultivation Stage?

Under the combined efforts of two great cultivators, they were lucky to slaughter the Sand Wolves to near extinction.

“Master...”

“Just call me Meng Jingzhou, and this is my junior brother, Lu Yang.”

“Ah? You, You two are Buddhist Meng and Sword Immortal Lu?” Old An and the group of merchants had not expected that their saviors were the legendary figures Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang, and they became excited.

These were legendary figures, and even in Great Xia, there weren’t many who had seen them; to think they would encounter them in Buddha Country.

This must be the so-called fateful connection spoken of by Buddhism.

“Indeed, it is us.” Meng Jingzhou kept a straight face, trying hard to maintain a detached demeanor, not wanting to let these merchants think that he was pleased by such a big reaction from them.

In the course of their conversation, Lu Yang learned that Old An was the leader of the merchants, named An Hu, and they had brought a consignment of solar lamps from Great Xia to see if there was a market for them in Buddha Country, never expecting to run into the Sand Wolves.

“Oh, you’re also going to Kaihuang City? If Uncle An doesn’t mind, could you perhaps take the two of us with you?”

Lu Yang thought to himself that good deeds indeed bring good rewards; what a coincidence this was.

“That would be great,” An Hu and the others said joyfully upon hearing this. To travel with legendary figures would give them face among other merchants.

And with these two individuals with them, there would certainly be no danger along the way.

Then, on the way to Kaihuang City, An Hu and the others encountered the Sand Wolf King out for vengeance having reached the Consummation of Qi Refinement, the notorious bandits of the Foundation Establishment Stage of the desert, a Golden Core Stage Demon Monk who had fallen onto the Demon Path to prove his way through killing, and the Nascent Soul Stage Lady Whitebone, born from a pile of dead bodies and sucking the essence blood of humans every night.

“You ordinary people have it quite tough being merchants.” Lu Yang remarked. The enemies they encountered on the road meant nothing to him and Old Meng, but for Old An and the others, they were calamities capable of wiping them out.

“...Actually, many merchants never encounter Sand Wolves in their lifetime.”

As for the likes of the Sand Wolf King and the Desert’s Three Thieves, those were even more far-fetched tales; the Demon Monk and Lady Whitebone were beings they had never even heard of.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou rode on camels, their first time riding them, which was rather fun.

Tied to both sides of the camels were the spoils of their journey: Sand Wolf pelts, the Sand Wolf King’s pelt, the Desert’s Three Thieves’ Storage Rings, the Demon Monk’s Golden Core, glittering white bones...

These items held no value for Lu Yang and the others; for example, the spirit stones in the Desert’s Three Thieves’ Storage Rings together didn’t amount to as much as what Lu Yang earned in a single day, and inside the ring was a key to open a secret realm, which upon checking the books brought from the Scripture Pavilion, was found to be suitable for Foundation Establishment Stage practitioners—a place many of them sought to pick herbs and concoct elixirs to increase their chances of forming a golden core by twenty percent.

The Demon Monk had a human skin scroll that detailed the method for forming a false core, which was comparable to the early stage of a Golden Core, but made further advancement hopeless.

The two thought to give all these items to Old An and the others, but on second thought, given the dangerous environment in Buddha Country, there might be incidents of murder for loot, and Old An and his group might not be able to keep so many things. In the end, they decided to leave only the Sand Wolf pelts for Old An and his group.

“Are you two masters coming to Kaihuang City to attend the Buddha Bathing Festival?” Old An struck up a conversation along the way, finding after some contact that the two masters were as gentle and approachable as depicted in the storytelling, with no airs about them.

“Yes, we were invited by Kaihuang Temple to participate.”

“That’s wonderful.” Old An and the others were very happy to hear this. With these two masters attending the Buddha Bathing Festival, it was sure to make the event even more lively.

“Speaking of which, we were not familiar with Kaihuang Temple before this. After receiving the invitation, we only then got to know of such a place.”

Old An laughed: “It’s normal for the two masters not to know about it. It might be because Kaihuang Temple has changed its name. The temple wasn’t called this before.”

“What was it called before?”

“Erli Village Temple.”

Chapter 983: Chapter 982: When in Rome, Do as the Romans Do

Chapter 983 -982: When in Rome, Do as the Romans Do

With two cultivators at the Divinity Transformation Stage offering protection, Old An and his companions had returned to Kaihuang City unharmed and without experiencing any dangers.

Just as Kaihuang Temple was originally named Erli Village Temple, Kaihuang City used to be called Erli Village, originally just an inconspicuous little place. Through the efforts of several generations of abbots from Kaihuang Temple, especially Master Duanchen, Erli Village was eventually developed into the sizeable and well-organized city it is today.

Unlike the cities of Great Xia, which were built using blue bricks and stone, the cities of Buddha Country generally used thick earthen walls. Weathered by the elements, their edges had been smoothed by wind and sun, giving them the appearance of being on the verge of collapse.

In actuality, the earthen walls’ interlayers were fortified with various array methods for stability and defense, ensuring that the city walls would stand for a thousand years.

An unnamed river flowed through Kaihuang City, providing the source of water for the entire city, and it was said to have been directed there by Master Duanchen as well.

Along the way, Lu Yang also saw many monks, with shaved heads and bare shoulders and arms, their skin dark and ruddy. As they walked, they perused scriptures, evidently devout believers, which made Lu Yang very concerned for their eyes.

Upon entering Kaihuang City, the differences from the cities of Great Xia became even more pronounced. There were beauties with blonde hair and blue eyes of exotic charm, with seductive figures and veils over their faces. There were ascetics with small monkeys perched on their shoulders. There were snake charmers who could make snakes dance by playing flutes. And there were fishmongers who placed knives vertically on the cutting board and then pressed fishes against the upright blades, avoiding taking life.

“Finally, no more sand.” Meng Jingzhou let out a sigh of relief. The pervasive sandstorm was too bothersome, but the city walls had a sand-blocking array method, which stopped the sand from entering and made things much more comfortable.

But Lu Yang’s spiritual space was not so fortunate.

In the spiritual space, sand was everywhere, forming undulating hillocks. A female immortal in golden exotic attire hummed a song and danced gracefully, her bare feet pressing into the sandy ground, leaving a trail of small footprints.

“Fairy, can you reduce the amount of sand a bit?” Lu Yang shouted, straining his voice. He was too far from Fairy Eternity; she wouldn’t hear him otherwise.

It was with great difficulty that they arrived in the city. Although there was no sand in reality, there was now sand in his spiritual space.

Fairy Eternity, twisting her waist, came up to Lu Yang, “This Immortal is just adapting to local customs. Look at you and the Meng Family Kid; you dress differently than the locals, and people have been staring at you continuously. If you look at me now, aren’t I less conspicuous?”

Lu Yang had long noticed the peculiar glances from passersby. Just like monks from Buddha Country would attract attention in Great Xia, he and Old Meng stood out noticeably as they walked down the main streets of the city.

They’d wanted to find a place where each could change into Buddha Country attire, but an appropriate opportunity had not yet presented itself.

Lu Yang glanced at Fairy Eternity, who was still dancing, and his face turned red as he quickly lowered his gaze. It was hard for the fairy to not attract attention this way; he didn’t even know where to look.

“Would the two masters care to come and sit at my humble abode?” Old An and his companions were very grateful to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou and wanted to entertain the two. If not for their protection, they would have fallen prey to the sand wolves long ago.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou declined Old An’s kind offer, got directions to Kaihuang Temple, and set off to visit it.

“Brother, walk faster!”

As Lu Yang approached the corner, suddenly a young girl ran over and bumped into him while looking back at her brother.

Before she collided with him, Lu Yang used a magic skill to gently wrap the girl in a breeze, stabilizing her so that she neither bumped into anyone nor fell.

“I’m sorry, I’m so sorry.” Realizing that she had nearly offended a cultivator, the girl quickly apologized.

Seeing this, the girl’s brother hurried over, “Sorry, it was my fault for not looking after my sister properly.”

“Be more careful when walking,” Lu Yang said, not taking the matter to heart.

Looking at the retreating figures of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, the young man’s gaze carried a hint of vigilance, “People from Great Xia...”

“Strange, why was that kid so wary of us just now, and what’s with the ‘People from Great Xia’ comment?” Although Lu Yang had walked a good distance away, his Spirit Transformation Level hearing was astonishingly acute, and he could clearly catch the youth’s muttering as if spoken directly to him.

“Probably hasn’t seen Great Xia Cultivators before, or maybe he was harmed by one?” Meng Jingzhou shrugged nonchalantly as he spoke, neither of them taking the youth seriously.

Lu Yang and his companion strolled leisurely through half of Kaihuang City, ambling and sightseeing, taking in the local customs and scenery of Buddha Country. By the time they reached Kaihuang Temple, it was already evening.

The Kaihuang Temple looked magnificent, with red walls and gray tiles, and the incense was burning vigorously. The cauldrons at the temple entrance were filled with incense ash, with only a few sticks left burning.

“Benefactors, the temple is closing to visitors now. Please come again tomorrow,” the Young Monk politely barred them at the entrance.

Lu Yang handed over the letter sent to him by the Kaihuang Temple to the Young Monk, “Please tell Master Duanchen for me.”

Master Duanchen was the abbot of Kaihuang Temple.

“Certainly.”

Before long, a white-haired monk hurried out from Kaihuang Temple, bustling along while chiding the Young Monk’s head, “I don’t know Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, and you still had the nerve to make me check the letter.”

“Benefactor Lu, Benefactor Meng, I’ve long admired you. I am the monk Duanchen,” greeted Master Duanchen with a smile brimming on his face and his hands pressed together. He had only hoped to try his luck, not really expecting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to come.

“So it’s Master Duanchen,” Lu Yang and his companion replied, mimicking Duanchen’s gesture of pressing their hands together in return.

“Please come in, my fellow daoists,” Master Duanchen gestured welcomingly, inviting them into the temple.

“I didn’t expect the benefactors to arrive so early. I apologize for any lack of hospitality on our part,” said Master Duanchen. The Buddha Bathing Festival was still two months away, and he had thought that even if they were to come, it wouldn’t be this soon.

However, this was a positive development. With their early arrival, Kaihuang Temple had more time to spread the news of Lu Yang and his companion’s participation in the Buddha Bathing Festival. Surely, this would attract many more cultivators than expected, making the festival even more lively.

“No trouble at all, we were afraid of unexpected delays on the road, so we started our journey a bit earlier,” they responded.

Lu Yang changed the subject, “I’ve heard that Kaihuang City was originally known as Erli Village and that it was your temple’s continuous efforts that built this place into what it is now. Truly a remarkable feat of great merit.”

Master Duanchen waved off the compliment, “It’s not any great merit. It’s just that one of the abbots was the illegitimate son of a high monk from Western Paradise Temple. That high monk wanted his son to live a better life, so he continuously supported our temple in secret, allowing us to achieve today’s scale. It’s all thanks to the blessings of those who came before us.”

“That high monk eventually passed away, leaving behind many Shariputras. The abbot at the time went to Western Paradise Temple to dispute ownership of the Shariputras and was never heard from again.”

Chapter 984: Chapter 983: In Heaven and Earth, I Alone am Honored

Chapter 984 -983: In Heaven and Earth, I Alone am Honored

Lu Yang’s mouth twitched; the history of Kaihuang Temple’s prosperity was truly unexpected.

“Western Paradise Temple is an orthodox institution of Buddha Country, they probably wouldn’t resort to murder...”

Stroking his white beard, Master Duanchen said, “Monks do not take life, so the Abbot’s life should be without concern, but as for other treatments, that’s harder to say. Our Kaihuang Temple doesn’t have much connection with Western Paradise Temple, and we have no way to inquire about the whereabouts of that Abbot.”

“After that Abbot disappeared, the scale of Kaihuang Temple never changed—it lacked any ambition.”

“Once I became the Abbot, I made a grand vow to ensure the incense at Kaihuang Temple burned brightly, aiming for an average annual visitor count of ten million.”

“To fulfill this grand vow, I diligently worked and devised ways to expand the renown of Kaihuang Temple, to make Kaihuang City comparable to a great city, and to improve the lives of the city’s residents.”

“...Master, the grand vow you made seems quite detailed.”

“Of course, the two Benefactors must not have been to our Buddha Country before and do not know how we make grand vows. The vows made in our Buddha Country are always very precise—if one only vows for ‘incense burning brightly,’ how should the criteria be set?”

“What counts as incense burning brightly? Would it count if one day a million Benefactors suddenly visited, or if a Benefactor paid for all the temple’s incense offerings for a year, or if the temple caught fire and all the incense was lit? Would these count as incense burning brightly?”

“If the standard is not set, the grand vow is just talk and can never be fulfilled.”

“Master, your dedication to Kaihuang Temple is truly admirable.”

Master Duanchen laughed and said, “Monks do not lie. I am not so great. When the incense at Kaihuang Temple is thriving, I, as the Abbot, naturally reap plenty of benefits and can fulfill my grand vow; why wouldn’t I do it?”

As Lu Yang knew, the incense money gained by each temple was divided so that fifty percent was kept by them, thirty percent was used to craft the Buddha’s Golden Body, and twenty percent was handed over to Western Paradise Temple.

Cultivation could not do without wealth; the more incense burned at Kaihuang Temple, the more Spirit Stones Master Duanchen would obtain for his own cultivation.

Master Duanchen thought it was getting late and wanted to take Lu Yang and his companion to the guesthouse to rest, but Lu Yang felt it was a rare opportunity and suggested visiting the Mahavira Hall instead. He had only seen the Mahavira Hall constructed by Fairy Eternity in the Spiritual Space; he had yet to see one in reality.

Meng Jingzhou had also never been to the Mahavira Hall and agreed with Lu Yang’s suggestion.

Master Duanchen led Lu Yang and his companion into the Mahavira Hall, where the Golden Great Sun Tathagata Buddha Statue, wrought in gold, was positioned in the very center, with a smile suggesting it was picking a flower, imparting compassion to enlighten the people.

It was already night, and the Mahavira Hall was brilliantly lit; the Buddha statue reflected the candlelight’s glow, making it look extraordinarily sacred.

“What’s there to see in the Mahavira Hall? The one I built for you in the Spiritual Space is the most authentic,” Fairy Eternity pouted. As a founder of Buddhism, according to Buddhist scriptures, wherever she was considered the Mahavira Hall—holy and inviolable.

In the Spiritual Space, at the end of the desert, a Mahavira Hall rose from the ground, even more splendid than the one in Kaihuang Temple.

In the center of the Treasure Palace, Immortal Fairy, donning Zhu Hong eye shadow and dressed in Western fashion, knelt on one leg atop the Lotus Platform, with the other leg resting on her thigh, hands in prayer position, and enchanted all beings.

Lu Yang glanced at the Mahavira Hall in the Spiritual Space, then at the one in reality, and felt that the real one was more authentic.

“Master, I’ve heard that the Buddha Bathing Festival is a celebration of the Worldly Venerable’s birth?” On the way there, Lu Yang had thoroughly studied the origins of the Buddha Bathing Festival to avoid being clueless in Buddha Country and looking like a tourist.

“What Benefactor Lu said is correct. It is said that in Ancient Times, when the Worldly Venerable was born, he could walk immediately. With each foot stepping on a lotus flower, he pointed one hand to the sky and the other to the earth, declaring, ‘In the heavens above and on the earth below, only I am the honored one.'”

“To commemorate the birth of the Worldly Venerable, this day was designated as Buddha’s Birthday, and the activity of bathing the Buddha was organized.”
