Meng Jingzhou chimed in from the side, “In the heavens above and on the earth below, only I am the honored one. Such a domineering statement from the Worldly Venerable.”

Master Duanchen chuckled and spoke unhurriedly, “It’s not surprising that Benefactor Meng has this misunderstanding. Many people misinterpret these words, thinking the Worldly Venerable was an egotistical man, but this is not the case.”

“The deeper meaning of ‘I’ here refers to the ‘Buddha-nature’ inherent in all beings, the fundamental essence that pervades everywhere, the innately pure and complete ‘true self.’ It is what the Nirvana Sutra describes as the ‘I’ of ‘permanent, joyous, self, and purity.'”

“The Auspicious Response Sutra states, ‘In the heavens above and on the earth below, only I am the honored one. The three realms are all suffering, what is there to be joyful about?’ Clearly, the ‘honored one’ here mainly refers to the significant responsibility of alleviating the suffering of all sentient beings.”

“Thus, the original intent of this phrase is that the Worldly Venerable declared he was born with the mission to save beings, to help sentient beings escape the sea of birth and death. When sentient beings become Buddhas, they too must do the same.”

Listened as Master Duanchen quoted scriptures to help him understand the phrase, texts he had never heard of before, Meng Jingzhou nodded repeatedly, realizing he had misunderstood the Worldly Venerable.

In the Spiritual Space, the Immortal Fairy Eternity standing on the Lotus Platform scratched her head at these words.

“Ah? Wasn’t this something I said in the tone of the Yingtian Immortal after I defeated him and the other three immortals? I thought it was quite domineering and described my abilities well, so I insisted they include it in the Buddhist scriptures when they were compiled, to declare that I was the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals.”

“So this phrase had such a meaning as well?”

Meng Jingzhou clasped his hands in salute, “I never expected the Worldly Venerable to have such compassion for the world, it was my misunderstanding of him.”

Master Duanchen smiled faintly, “The Worldly Venerable indeed possesses great wisdom, great determination, and a great compassionate heart. I wonder if Benefactor Meng has heard that when the Worldly Venerable was seeking Enlightenment under the Bodhi Tree, the demon Mara sent three demonesses to seductively distract him. The Worldly Venerable was not swayed by the demonesses; he attained Enlightenment in seven days, reaching the Consummation of Enlightenment and developing great wisdom.”

“After the Worldly Venerable attained Enlightenment, his Buddha light shone for miles, illuminating worlds in all directions, and even the Four Ancient Immortals came to congratulate him.”

“There is such a tale.” Previously, Meng Jingzhou had not much exposure to Buddhism, but now hearing Master Duanchen recount the past of the Worldly Venerable, he felt true admiration.

“Speaking of the Bodhi Tree, I once felt my culinary skills had reached their peak and decided to compile the ‘Culinary Bible’ to bless future generations. While composing the book under the Bodhi Tree, Xiao Ling, Lianyi, and Qinghe always liked to hover around me, insisting that I play with them and disrupting my writing.”

“Strangely enough, I remember that the three of them had to leave for some reason and should not have been there. Was it an illusion conjured by someone, or perhaps an Inner Demon?”

“Regardless, my willpower was resolute, and unaffected by their interference, I managed to complete the ‘Culinary Bible’ in seven days.”

“Then Immortal Jiuchong came over with several Golden Crows, their brightness unbearable, almost setting the freshly written book ablaze. Later, Yingtian Immortal and the other two came one after another to congratulate me, seeing them laugh so joyfully, they all seemed overcome with tears.”

While watching Meng Jingzhou chat merrily with Master Duanchen, Lu Yang considered whether or not to tell his good brother the true story of the Worldly Venerable.

Chapter 985: Chapter 984: Master, I Have Understood

Chapter 985 -984: Master, I Have Understood

Lu Yang could tell that the Four Ancient Immortals were trying their best to glorify Fairy Eternity, and the effects were significant. Even Old Meng thought after listening that Fairy Eternity was a true Buddha of great virtue, admiring her endlessly.

“Forget it, let’s not talk about it anymore,” said Lu Yangxin, too kind-hearted to set up his good friend, “It’s better to keep the true facts of ancient times to oneself. It’s enough that Old Meng is with me when he Passes Tribulation.”

After visiting the Mahavira Hall, Master Duanchen led them to the guest rooms.

The walls of the guest room were inscribed with wild cursive scriptures written by Master Duanchen himself, infused with Essence, Qi, and Spirit. Lu Yang couldn’t understand them at all, but he felt that, even without understanding, just being in the room provided a tranquility that calmed the spirit, helping cultivators enter a Meditative Trance quickly.

Writing scriptures on the walls was a significant expenditure for Master Duanchen, impossible to replicate in every guest room.

“This must be one of the best guest rooms in Kaihuang Temple, though it’s of little use to me.”

Lu Yang sat on the bed and entered into Meditative Trance within a few moments.

He had long suffered from the interference of Immortal Fairy, and as long as he avoided listening to her speak, he could enter Meditative Trance at any time.

He cultivated throughout the night.

Lu Yang came out of the Meditative Trance, opened the door to his room, and stretched comfortably, feeling refreshed and clear-headed.

The neighboring room’s door opened, and Meng Jingzhou woke up too.

“Hei—Ha—”

Hearing the uniform shout of “Hei-Ha” nearby, they followed the sound and saw the monks of Kaihuang Temple practicing their boxing during the morning exercise; their movements were synchronized, and their voices thunderous.

“Do you recognize what martial art this is?” Lu Yang asked, as he was not very knowledgeable about martial arts.

“It should be Long Arm Boxing,” Meng Jingzhou observed carefully and replied, “It’s a form of folk martial arts that stretches the muscles and tendons, strengthening the body.”

Kaihuang Temple housed many mundane monks who could not learn Cultivation Techniques and could only practice folk martial arts.

Though it was folk martial arts, its effectiveness was in no way inferior to low-level Cultivation Techniques. There were records in the martial arts world of many masters defeating Qi Cultivation Stage Cultivators.

For example, initially, Long Arm Boxing was just a very ordinary martial art with nothing special about it. However, everything changed after the founder of Long Arm Boxing kindly saved an old beggar who was being bullied by thugs and treated him to a meal.

Upon waking the next day, the founder found a brand new Long Arm Boxing manual placed by his pillow, which had enhanced the existing foundations making it easier to learn, quick to cultivate, and raised its upper limits.

The thirty-sixth generation successor of Long Arm Boxing had a similar experience, inadvertently forming a good relationship with a great Cultivation Power, which transformed Long Arm Boxing once again.

It is said that a great power capable of Passing Tribulation once roamed the mortal world as an ordinary child, learning and enhancing Long Arm Boxing.

Such instances made Long Arm Boxing, though still a folk martial art, far more powerful than it originally was.

Similar experiences happened more or less with other folk martial arts, all having had some exposure to immortal fates.

“The rumors that Long Arm Boxing was modified by a great power able to Pass Tribulation must be true,” Meng Jingzhou said. With his insight, he couldn’t spot any aspects of Long Arm Boxing that could be modified without disrupting its integrity, indicating that the Cultivator who modified Long Arm Boxing had a Cultivation Level far beyond his own.

“Good morning, Benefactors,” Master Duanchen appeared behind them with a smile, holding a string of Buddha Beads.

“Master.”

“May I know what the Benefactors have planned for today? It will help me arrange things properly,” he asked.

Lu Yang smiled and said, “We’ve just arrived and know very little about Buddha Country, so we have no specific plans. We leave it all to you, Master.”

“Today is the day I receive pilgrims, which can also be considered a major feature of our temple. If the two benefactors are free, why not come and see?”

As the abbot, Master Duanchen has numerous responsibilities and couldn’t possibly meet with pilgrims every day; otherwise, he would accomplish nothing.

Therefore, he established a rule to randomly receive pilgrims on one day within the month, depending entirely on fate.

“Then we will impose upon the master.”

The incense offerings at Kaihuang Temple were more prosperous than under the previous abbots, with many pilgrims waiting at the door even before it opened, including some from other cities.

When the pilgrims learned that today was the day Master Duanchen would be receiving them, they were overjoyed.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had special identities. Although not everyone knew their faces, their reputations were well known. If someone recognized them, news would likely spread, and pilgrims would swarm to Kaihuang Temple.

Thus, the two concealed their forms and Qi, standing beside Master Duanchen.

Receiving pilgrims involved enlightening them and resolving their worries and troubles.

The first pilgrim was a delicately frail woman, weak as if a gust of wind could blow her over, weeping incessantly.

“Master, many years ago, my fiancé ran away with my maid on our wedding night. I tried to let it go, but after so many years, I simply cannot forget him.”

Master Duanchen smiled faintly, took out a Jade Vase, and filled it with water.

“Female benefactor, look. This Jade Vase is you. To let go of someone, you need to fill yourself with new things to replace that person.”

“Master, I have understood.”

“Initially, the water in the vase would gradually dry up, but you kept thinking about him, making the water in the vase increase instead of focusing on other things.”

The second pilgrim was a rather forthright woman, though she couldn’t help but reveal her sadness when discussing the past.

“Master, I had a childhood friend with whom I shared everything. Times were hard, and to make ends meet, my father sold me to the Yuan family to be a personal maid to the young mistress. Then one day, I saw the fiancé of the young mistress, who was my childhood friend. He took me away on the mistress’s wedding night, intending to wander the world with me, but shortly after our marriage, he said he wanted to renounce worldly attachments and join Buddhism. So many years have passed, and I still cannot forget him.”

Master Duanchen smiled faintly, took out a Jade Vase filled with water, and poured out the water.

“Female benefactor, have you understood?”

The second pilgrim seemed pensive: “Spilled water is hard to regain. My husband’s departure is an unchangeable reality, and I need to accept this fact and move forward. Master, I have understood.”

The third pilgrim was a wandering monk with a darkened face, seemingly from long periods of wandering.

“Master, my cultivation has reached a bottleneck.

“I had a fiancée and a childhood friend, both wonderful girls. I chose my childhood friend, and after getting married, suddenly one day, as I was with my childhood friend, I had an epiphany: familial and romantic love are emotions that bind me. I felt everything was meaningless; perhaps Buddhism was calling me. I left my childhood friend and became a wandering monk. Yet, after so many years, I feel increasingly unsuited for seclusion. Please, master, resolve my doubts.”

Master Duanchen smiled faintly and used magic skills to gather the water on the ground back into the Jade Vase.

The third pilgrim suddenly had a realization: “Master, does this mean there’s a chance to make amends? Can I return to secular life?”

Master Duanchen then hit the pilgrim over the head with the vase, knocking him out.

“I find it satisfying to hit people like this.”

Before losing consciousness, the pilgrim vaguely saw Master Duanchen flipping over a table and quickly opened the door to call out to the first two pilgrims who were about to leave: “Two female benefactors, hold off on letting go!”

Chapter 986: Chapter 985: Could My Brother Have Been Possessed?

Chapter 986 -985: Could My Brother Have Been Possessed?

Master Duanchen gathered the three pilgrims in a side hall, letting them mutter about their own affairs, no longer concerning himself with them.

“I’ve caused the two benefactors some amusement,” Master Duanchen said with an apologetic smile, “usually, a poor monk like myself would not lift a hand in receiving pilgrims.”

That made sense, they had known each other since childhood, Cui Que’er was quite beautiful and kind-hearted, having a crush on her was nothing out of the ordinary.

Just as Lu Yang was about to tease them with a laugh, he suddenly heard a bang. The wooden door shattered, and several mysterious people clad in black robes burst into Tang Qiaoqiao’s home.

The hems of their black robes were painted with a red skull symbol.

Tang Chuanwu recognized the skull symbol, his expression dramatically changed, "People from the Skull Divine Sect!"

The leader let out an inhuman laugh, lifted his hood, and revealed a face swollen as if soaked in water.

"Boy, I am Protector Jiao of the Skull Divine Sect’s Twenty-Eight Constellations. You took something from my sect, did you think hiding it here would keep us from finding it?"

Protector Jiao licked his lips, surveyed Lu Yang and the others, who were just frail mortals.

"You tell me, hand it over willingly and we’ll let you keep a full corpse, or should I slaughter you all?"

Tang Chuanwu inwardly cursed his luck; despite his extreme caution, he had still been found by the Skull Divine Sect.

Cultivators truly possessed all kinds of incredible Divine Abilities!

Lu Yang’s mind was full of questions. What was the Skull Divine Sect, and why had he never heard of it?

Tang Chuanwu only regretted that his age prevented him from cultivating; otherwise, he would not have been so passive in the face of cultivators, knowing so little about their methods. His only option was to continue to practice martial arts to strengthen himself.

Three months ago, he left the city to gather herbs. Since the journey to the collection site was so far, requiring a full day for a round trip, herbal apprentices usually stayed at the site for two or three days, and Tang Chuanwu was no exception.

He found an oasis to rest, and the first day passed without incident. However, on the second night, a person stumbled into the oasis, seriously wounded and bleeding profusely, clinging to a wooden box until death, eyeing him warily.

He did not want to stir up trouble and sensed that something significant had occurred, so without regard for the dangers of night travel, he prepared to leave.

But before he could leave, black-robed individuals bearing the mark of the Skull Divine Sect surrounded the oasis. Worried that Tang Chuanwu might leak their secrets, they used magic, causing his bones to grow rapidly within his body, piercing his flesh and heart, and killing him.

In his second reincarnation, Tang Chuanwu waited until the man died, opened the wooden box, and found an unknown elixir and a small fragment. He planned to take the elixir and flee, but it was a step too late—the black-robed individuals surrounded the oasis again, killing him.

In the third reincarnation, Tang Chuanwu immediately swallowed the elixir upon finding it. Agonizing pain sent him into unconsciousness, and while he was out, the black-robed individuals killed him.

In the fourth reincarnation, Tang Chuanwu disregarded the wooden box, planning to escape back to Kaihuang City at dawn. Unfortunately, the black-robed people had already set up an extensive encirclement nearby, preventing anyone from leaving the region. His escape failed, and he died.

In the fifth reincarnation, he broke out of the encirclement only to die in a sudden sandstorm.

The sixth, the seventh...

Tang Chuanwu kept reincarnating until he finally understood the whole story. These black-robed individuals were members of the Skull Divine Sect, all cultivators, their influence spread across the nearby eight cities, terribly fearsome.

Among them, one member coveted the treasures of the Divine Sect, stealing a Marrow Cleansing Pill and a fragment of mysterious origin, exceptionally sharp.

In the last reincarnation, he ambushed the one who had stolen the treasures.

The man was already gravely wounded, and combined with the Long Arm Boxing technique he had pilfered from the Kaihuang Temple, along with the familiarity of combat routines from previous reincarnations, he killed the man and seized the wooden box, swallowed the Marrow Cleansing Pill, and after regaining consciousness, broke through the encirclement.

The Skull Divine Sect’s men wanted to pursue him but were thrown into disarray by the sandstorm.

His body became stronger after the Marrow Cleansing Pill, and having prepared for the sandstorm, he finally escaped with his life.

Unexpectedly, three months later, he was still found by members of the Skull Divine Sect.

This is troublesome. He heard that the Constellation Protectors of the Twenty-Eight Constellations were all major figures at the Consummation of Qi Refinement. A direct confrontation was definitely not an option. He wondered how many times he would have to die before he could deal with Protector Jiao.

Tang Chuanwu’s mind raced with plans for the next reincarnation. The Buddha Bathing Festival would begin in ten days. Many cultivators from other regions were already entering Kaihuang City. Perhaps he could use these foreign cultivators to engage Protector Jiao. However, only cultivators at the Foundation Establishment Stage could fight Protector Jiao, and such cultivators were not easy to find.

Moreover, he heard that the Master of the Skull Divine Sect was a Nascent Soul Elder, whose every move could cause extraordinary phenomena, and who was incredibly powerful, mastering over a hundred magic skills. Even if he got past this obstacle, how would he deal with the Divine Sect Master later on?

Wait, it seems that this time, reincarnation isn’t necessary.

Tang Chuanwu turned his head to look at Master Lu, who was deep in thought, and Master Meng, who wore a puzzled expression.

Cui Que’er and Tang Qiaoqiao looked at Protector Jiao with strange eyes—confusion, curiosity, amusement... but no fear.

The sleeves of the black-robed person continually extended bones, rapidly spreading across the entire room. Sharp bone spurs were aimed at Lu Yang and the others; with just one command, the spurs would proliferate again, stabbing them into a hive!

"What’s the matter, not handing over the treasures yet? It seems you won’t shed tears until you see the coffin," Protector Jiao sneered continuously. After he killed, he would just leave, and even Kaihuang Temple would not trace his whereabouts.

Protector Jiao gave a signal and ordered his Left and Right Protectors, "Do it!"

"Do what? Can’t you see I’m in the middle of thinking?" Meng Jingzhou said impatiently as he stepped forward, ignoring the thorny bone spurs, letting them pierce his body.

Protector Jiao’s pupils shrank. The supposedly indestructible bone spurs broke upon contact, like foxtails, causing no harm whatsoever.

"This is impossible, who are you!" Protector Jiao shouted, sensing something was very wrong. This time he had hit an iron wall!

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t be bothered to talk. He released his imposing aura; with his natural commanding presence, Protector Jiao, and the others felt as if they were carrying the weight of mountains on their backs. They collapsed to the ground with a clang, bleeding from all seven orifices!

"You wouldn’t dare kill me. Mess with the Skull Divine Sect, and even if you run to the ends of the earth, we will kill you!"

"Don’t even think that everyone else is like me; I’m just the weakest of the twenty-eight Protectors!"

"Above the Twenty-Eight Constellations Protector, there are the Seven Luminaries Protector, Four Symbols Protector, Left and Right Protectors, the Holy Daughter and Son, and the mysterious and unfathomable leader of the..."

Lu Yang looked up, his eyes widening in realization, "I was wondering why your clothes looked so familiar. I’ve seen them before."

He pulled out a black robe from his identity jade pendant, the robe’s skull emblem woven with gold and silver thread, a testament to its exquisite craftsmanship.

Protector Jiao, upon seeing the black robe in Lu Yang’s hands, reacted as if he had seen a ghost, a boundless fear spreading in his heart, his voice uncontrollable, "This, this is the Master’s clothing!"

During his time as a Protector, he had the fortune of seeing Lady Whitebone seated amidst a mountain of corpses and a sea of blood, with countless blood and bone servants.

Lu Yang recalled the journey to Kaihuang City, "On the way to Kaihuang City, I happened to encounter a Bone Spirit who claimed to be Lady Whitebone, wanting to take Old Meng as a manservant. Old Meng casually disposed of her, so it turns out she was your Master."

If it wasn’t for the black-robed individual’s illustrious appearance, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou would have had little impression of Lady Whitebone, just another underling.

"How is this possible, the Master is an old Nascent Soul Early Stage cultivator who broke core to reach Nascent fifty years ago!" Protector Jiao still couldn’t believe it, that was an all-powerful Nascent Soul cultivator!

Lu Yang thought about it, that Lady Whitebone was indeed formidable; fifty years ago, he definitely would not have been able to defeat her.

"It’s unexpected that this Bone Spirit had subordinates, but since you’ve come, let’s wrap this up in one go."

Lu Yang turned to ask Tang Chuanwu and the others, "You don’t have plans this afternoon, do you? Would you like to join us in taking care of this Divine Sect? We’ll try to be quick so we can make it back in time for dinner."

Tang Chuanwu nodded stiffly, his brain struggling to keep up.

Tang Qiaoqiao and Cui Que’er, however, were quite excited; this was far more interesting than just running around in Kaihuang City.

Following the results of Protector Jiao’s Soul Search, Lu Yang and his companion headed straight for the lair of the Skull Divine Sect, and without any nonsense, they began a massacre.

"Who dares to intrude upon the Divine Sect..."

"Constellation Protector, save me..."

"Seven Luminaries Protector, save me..."

"Four Symbols Protector, save me..."

"Left and Right Protectors, save me..."

"Tang Qiaoqiao, as the clone I’ve cultivated..."

"If you dare to kill me, I will detonate the blood within Tang Qiaoqiao’s body..."

"Holy Daughter, save me..."

"Saint Heir, save me..."

"Phew, finally dealt with that." Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou fought their way through the Skull Divine Sect, eliminating six strongholds with incredible speed.

"Faster than expected."

"We killed them too quickly earlier. Speaking of which, doesn’t Tang Qiaoqiao look a bit like the Left Protector? Didn’t the Left Protector say something before he died?"

Meng Jingzhou shrugged his shoulders, "Probably something about a clone cultivated for Possession or the like. Not important, anyway; with the Left Protector gone, it’s better that the girl doesn’t know too much, or it might lead to psychological issues."

"That makes sense."

Tang Chuanwu was completely stunned throughout the ordeal, still unable to comprehend what had happened.

From the moment Protector Jiao broke into their home, Tang Chuanwu had braced himself to die dozens of times, to be caught in a cycle of Reincarnation, to survive in a constant state of peril, to match wits and courage against the Skull Divine Sect, perhaps even to uncover the mystery of his sister’s origins.

And yet, in just one afternoon, it was all resolved?

"This Skull Divine Sect has such a grand name, yet I haven’t seen anything of value,"

Lu Yang and another person brought Tang Chuanwu and his three people to scavenge the treasures of the Skull Divine Sect, but they didn’t find as much as the legacy left by the Three-eyed Ghost Monk and the Hollow Shadow.

While looting, Meng Jingzhou grumbled discontentedly, "Why would you call yourselves the Skull Divine Sect, making me think you’re on the same level as the Ruthless Sect and the Eternity Sect, about to catch a big fish, yet this is all there is?"

Lu Yang and the other were worldly, having seen much already, and there were few things that could catch their eye, but it was different for Tang Chuanwu and his three companions.

Any single item from the Skull Divine Sect was viewed by them as a treasure of considerable value.

For instance, the Marrow Cleansing Pill that Tang Chuanwu had taken before: Lu Yang had scrounged up several bottles, all of which were worthless trinkets.

A single drop of blood from him or Old Meng was more effective than the Marrow Cleansing Pill.

By the Divinity Transformation Stage, after many purifications of impurities, their bodies had become as natural as those born from the earth, free of any impurity, and their blood, flesh, and bones contained an exceedingly terrifying amount of spiritual essence, precious treasures to any Qi Refinement or Foundation Establishment cultivator.

Not to mention Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou; their physiques had even reached the Body Integration Realm level, even more terrifying.

"Right, that Protector Jiao mentioned you took something of theirs, what did you take?"

Tang Chuanwu was conflicted, uncertain whether to tell Lu Yang and the other person the truth. The Marrow Cleansing Pill wasn’t a big deal, but that artifact shard was no ordinary item. Although its origins were unknown, it was incredibly sharp, definitely not ordinary.

Although Lu Yang and his companion had far-reaching reputations, what if they were tempted by wealth? ƒгeewёbnovel.com

He gritted his teeth and decided to try, thinking that even if they were tempted by wealth, he could start over.

"Once, when I was out gathering medicinal herbs, I happened upon people from the Skull Divine Sect and got a wooden box from a dying man. There was Marrow Cleansing Pill and an artifact shard inside the box."

"An artifact shard?"

"I’ve hidden it somewhere else, not on me," admitted Tang Chuanwu. He was worried that the people from the Skull Divine Sect would search him and find the shard on him directly. If the shard was kept elsewhere, he could buy some time.

"May I take a look?" Lu Yang was primarily concerned that the shard might be some dangerous item that could pose a risk to Tang Chuanwu.

After dealing with the Skull Divine Sect, the group followed Tang Chuanwu to a large banyan tree within Kaihuang City.

Tang Chuanwu briskly retrieved the artifact shard from a bird’s nest in the tree. The shard had complex patterns on its inner side, indicative of some unknown Array Method.

Lu Yang scanned the artifact shard with his Spiritual Sense and consulted with the fairy, soon coming to a conclusion: "It looks like a part of a cauldron, the main material being Sky Star Copper. The complete cauldron must be a magic artifact of a Pass Tribulation Cultivator."

Meng Jingzhou looked at Lu Yang in surprise. You, kid, are not supposed to know Refining, yet you could discern so much?

A small force like the Skull Divine Sect, with a leader only at the Nascent Soul Early Stage, could not possibly possess anything belonging to a Pass Tribulation Cultivator, not even a shard.

"It’s likely an artifact obtained by a stroke of luck; even the Skull Divine Sect themselves didn’t know the origins of this object."

Lu Yang handed the shard back to Tang Chuanwu: "Keep it, this shard has some history. It’s a nice find. If you can locate the other pieces, they should automatically assemble into the complete cauldron."

A Tribulation-Passing Level magic artifact, nothing worth making a fuss over, as long as it was not dangerous.

Tang Chuanwu carefully stored it away. This was a fragment of a powerful magic artifact from a Pass Tribulation Cultivator, incredibly valuable. If he was lucky enough to find the other fragments in the future, he might even obtain the complete cauldron.

"Then, please, Miss Cui, lead us to a place to dine."

Lu Yang and his companion were in such a hurry to deal with the Skull Divine Sect just to make it in time for a meal.

As night fell, Kaihuang City remained bustling. Cui Que’er led everyone to a lavish tavern adorned with colorful lights.

"Here we are."

Then Lu Yang and the others enjoyed a high-end congee.

Lu Yang really wanted to say, "Can’t you guys from Buddha Country come up with a different way? This stuff looks completely unappetizing."

"I even promised to bring Sister Mengmeng some specialties from Buddha Country; I can’t just bring back a bucket of slop, can I?"

Although the upscale slop wasn’t much to look at, it actually tasted quite good and wasn’t as hard to swallow as what he had eaten at noon.

After the meal, Cui Que’er, as promised, took Lu Yang and company on a tour of Kaihuang City, with the Tang siblings laughing and chatting by their side.

"Alright, it’s about time we headed back," said Lu Yang. Kaihuang City was very big, and one evening was certainly not enough to see it all.

He and Old Meng had plenty of energy to keep walking, but Cui Que’er and her companions did not. Their energy was limited.

Fearing any accidents on the way back, Lu Yang escorted each of them home one by one.

"We’ll be staying at Kaihuang Temple for a while longer, so if anything comes up, feel free to come find me."

Before parting ways, Lu Yang thought for a moment, then flicked his index finger, sending out three drops of blood into the hands of the three of them.

"I can’t let you introduce us around Kaihuang City for nothing. These three drops of blood can serve as payment. They’re more useful than Marrow Cleansing Pills. Remember to dilute them with water, otherwise your bodies won’t be able to take it," he said.

Old Meng’s blood wasn’t something to give away lightly due to its strong side effects, but Lu Yang’s blood didn’t have that concern.

"See you later."

Western Paradise Temple.

Meng Junzi triumphantly held the recently captured remnants of the Ruthless Sect, showing off in front of Abbot Master Mingyu.

"What did I tell you? With the Meng Family joining Buddha Country, we were bound to find people from the Ruthless Sect," he boasted.

Master Mingyu twitched at the corner of his eyes, admittedly having to concede that, ever since the Meng Family had joined Buddha Country and worked with the monks from Western Paradise Temple to hunt for the Ruthless Sect, the results had indeed been considerable. Was this the umpteenth Ruthless Sect Elder they had captured?

"Well done, I did not expect Benefactor Meng to take action personally," said Master Mingyu.

He had assumed that, being an Immortal of legend, Meng Junzi would maintain his dignity and not get involved, leaving the task to the younger members of the Meng Family.

Yet here he was, acting personally.

Meng Junzi threw the remnant of the Ruthless Sect aside carelessly and sat down boldly: "Little Ming, that’s what you don’t understand. I didn’t act before because I had to deceive Guan Shanhai. Now that we’ve captured Guan Shanhai, isn’t it time for me to make an appearance in the world?"

Master Mingyu joined his hands, saying nothing further.

The monks had already reported to him the details of Meng Junzi’s capture. It was indeed quite a spectacle.

When Meng Junzi captured the Ruthless Sect Elder, he displayed all manner of miracles between Heaven and Earth, as if the whole world had become his domain. People throughout the city knelt in worship, shouting praises of the Worldly Venerable’s divine presence.

At that moment, the Ruthless Sect Elder’s mind went blank. No matter how evil he was, he did not expect an Immortal to come after him personally.

Normally, those sent to capture him would have cultivation levels similar to his. But instead, it jumped straight past the Pass Tribulation Cultivator and Semi-Immortal stages. There was no need for such a force to capture a sect master!

As Meng Junzi recalled the reaction of the people throughout the city, a smile crept up his lips uncontrollably.

After enduring for a hundred thousand years, he was finally able to act openly and righteously.

All that talk about Immortals maintaining their dignity and rarely acting was nonsense.

Hadn’t he painstakingly cultivated all these years just for this moment?

"All thanks to the opportunity given by Junior Brother Yun Zhi," he said.

```

If one were to speak of the most dazzling figure in Buddha Country nowadays, it would be none other than Meng Junzi, who yearned for Buddhist teachings and harbored good intentions, having just joined Buddha Country.

Meng Junzi, in order to capture the followers of the Ruthless Sect, showcased his divine might in Buddha Country, commanding an aura of authority. Even in Buddha Country, where communication was not convenient, the news still spread throughout the land at an incredibly fast pace.

By comparison, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s participation in the Buddha Bathing Festival in Kaihuang City was simply a piece of news circulating among a few cities, hardly noticeable.

The more Meng Junzi thought about it, the more he saw Daoist Yun Zhi as a junior brother with great potential, who had provided him with such a good opportunity just by coming to Buddha Country.

"If it weren’t for Daoist Yun Zhi keeping such a close watch, I would’ve done whatever it took to pull him into our Meng Family."

"Forget it, I don’t want to think about these things anymore." Meng Junzi shook his head, casting away the unhappy troubles and determined to fully enjoy life in Buddha Country.

"Then Little Ming, carry on with your work, I’ll continue with my captures." Meng Junzi really enjoyed the feeling of being worshipped, it was quite intoxicating.

The last time he had this sort of treatment was ten thousand years ago when he was waging wars across the land.

Master Mingyu saw it clearly, Meng Junzi was truly devoted to capturing followers of the Ruthless Sect and showing off his sanctity in front of others as a side benefit.

That was good, it kept him from always staying in our Western Paradise Temple, lest he discover the real backing of the temple and cause unnecessary chaos.

Celestial King City, one of the twelve top-tier cities in Buddha Country, and its Abbot of Celestial King Temple possessed Mid-stage Transcendance Tribulation Stage cultivation level, with profound Buddhist teachings and extraordinary strength.

Dark clouds loomed over the city, and heavy rain poured down. Meng Junzi arrived in Celestial King City, walking in the rain without getting wet, and reminiscing about the memories gained from a Soul Search.

Ever since Daoist Buyu had a breakthrough to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage and captured one of the vice sect hierarchs of the Ruthless Sect, Great Xia had been actively hunting down Ruthless Sect members, to the point where the sect’s lower and middle ranks were completely annihilated, leaving only the upper echelons struggling to survive.

Fearing being wiped out by Great Xia in one fell swoop, the high ranks of the Ruthless Sect also adopted a one-way communication method, with orders passed down from the Master to the vice sect hierarchs and from the vice sect hierarchs to the Elders.

However, there were occasional private exchanges between Elders for various reasons.

From the memories of a captured Elder of the Ruthless Sect, Meng Junzi learned that there was an Elder of the Ruthless Sect hiding in Celestial King City.

"I’ll choose here."

Meng Junzi turned into an alleyway, where at the end there was a shabby little shop with no name.

Based on Meng Junzi’s experience in searching for gourmet food, the more remote and dilapidated the place, such as this little shop, the more likely it was to find astonishingly divine delicacies.

Meng Junzi informed several elders of the Meng Family via mental communication, "You guys lead them to me later; don’t worry about what happens next."

"Understood!" several elders from the Meng Family responded in unison via mental communication.

Meng Junzi walked into the shop with a smile. Unlike the dirty exterior, the interior of the shop was clean and tidy, creating a comfortable atmosphere.

He looked around the shop and did not see a menu, which convinced him even more that the shopkeeper must be an expert.

"Shopkeeper, what are the specialties here?" Meng Junzi shouted toward the kitchen.

Upon hearing a customer, the cooking maid in a grey skirt lifted the curtain and walked out of the kitchen with a ladle in hand.

Meng Junzi was taken aback when he saw the cooking maid. ƒreewebnσvel.com

The cooking maid had delicate features, as if meticulously sculpted by an expert, her beauty was breathtaking.

Meng Junzi was secretly astonished to find such a beauty in a modest place, even the woman known as the number one beauty of the world ten thousand years ago, Zhui Yue, paled in comparison to this cooking maid. Only Daoist Yun Zhi could match her beauty.

And like Daoist Yun Zhi, she had an indifferent demeanor, radiating a ’do not disturb’ aura.

Meng Junzi chuckled to himself; it was also rather pleasing to demonstrate his sanctity in front of such a beautiful cooking maid.

"Shopkeeper, do you have a menu here?"

"No, I cook whatever comes to mind. Do you want to eat?" asked the cooking maid, without a trace of warmth towards the rare customer, her tone cold and distant.
```

"Alright." The cooking maid didn’t say much, turning around to enter the kitchen, soon followed by the clanging sounds of chopping vegetables.

Before long, a fragrant aroma wafted from the kitchen, as the cooking maid brought out a plate of gruel and a bowl of rice.

The fragrance originated from this gruel.

Meng Junzi straightened his back slightly to show his respect for the delicious food, having tasted many gruels, none smelled as appetizing as this one.

Meng Junzi took a spoonful of gruel, grimaced, and spat it out.

The heavy rain continued, and the Ruthless Sect Elder Bai Hun frantically sprinted through the rain cursing his luck.

```
"A Dao Fruit of absorption?"
```

```
Meng Junzi also became irate—he was an Immortal who had fought his way out of the blood seas of the late Great Yu era, having even defeated the Great Yu National Preceptor, Guan Shanhai. In terms of combat power, he feared no one.
```

```
"Thousand Hammer Glazed Body!"

```

```

Meng Junzi’s body was covered in a lustrous sheen, shimmering brilliantly in the sunlight. This was his personal Body Refining Technique, forged through thousands of poundings and having withstood tens of thousands of Thunder Tribulations, not even Jiang Pingan would dare to fight him bare-handed in this state.

```

```
Unmoved by the irate Meng Junzi, Ashy Bean pointed one hand to the heavens and one to the earth, uttering the sacred words, "Above and below the heavens, I alone am honored."
```

```
"Immortal Killing Fist!"

```

Ashy Bean looked down upon all beings, staring at the mortal world with a hegemon’s poise, a sense of invincibility about her, as if despite the unparalleled geniuses enduring countless hardships to ascend to immortality, none compared to her!

Her punch was peerless, the earth and sky changed colors at its release, the immense and limitless power of the Annihilation Dao Fruit poured entirely into her fist.

She believed she was invincible; to fight using any Immortal Artifact would be a blasphemy to her own strength.

Boom—

Above the clouds, countless roaring sounds erupted as if over a thousand True Dragons were bellowing, deafening to the ears.

"Pfft—"

The glazed body shattered, and Meng Junzi’s chest caved in directly; he hadn’t anticipated that Ashy Bean’s fist would be so formidable, his prized Thousand Hammer Glazed Body entirely incapable of withstanding it!

"Borrowing Injury!"

Meng Junzi used the Borrowing Dao Fruit, forcibly transferring his injuries to Ashy Bean.

Ashy Bean’s chest felt as though she had hammered it herself, equally severely wounded.

This move had been used during the Imperial City battle against Guan Shanhai, who kept repairing his injuries and fell into a passive state.

However, Ashy Bean did not intend to heal her wounds, continuing to fight with her injured body, her combat power undiminished.

Meng Junzi was shocked beyond measure, could it be that his opponent had seen through the flaws of this move?

With the Borrowing Dao Fruit, a loan had to be repaid; after a period of time, the injuries would automatically return, and with interest at that, making the returned injuries even heavier.

Guan Shanhai had not realized this, blindly healing his injuries to avoid the situation of them returning.

How had his opponent managed to figure this out?

Ashy Bean had not figured it out; she merely felt that she should not heal, a judgment born from her combat instincts.

The two ascended from the clouds to space, where the illusory shadows of stars trembled in the aftermath of the dueling immortals.

"Drawing strength from the past and future!"

Two figures crossed the long river of Suiyue, arriving from the past and the future to fight alongside Meng Junzi.

Together, these two figures were equivalent to another Meng Junzi, doubling his combat power.

Yet in front of Ashy Bean, even if the Four Ancient Immortals themselves arrived, she would not fear them, let alone whether it was one Meng Junzi or two; there wasn’t much difference.

"Destroy the concept of ’time’."

In an instant, the entire world plunged into chaos, losing the concept of time. The figures of Meng Junzi from the past and future crumbled away, and then the concept of time was restored.

Meng Junzi felt as if he was facing Yun Zhi herself, utterly without the ability to fight back, as Ashy Bean’s consecutive punches left him battered and bruised.

"Dissolve!"

Meng Junzi dared not linger in battle any longer, using an Escape Skill, leaving behind a self-detonating clone, while his true form fled precipitously.

Boom—

The entire area exploded into a vacuum, even the shadows of the stars disappearing.

Ashy Bean brushed away the self-detonation dust, looking toward Meng Junzi’s vanishing figure, she sensed for a moment and discovered that no causality had formed between them.

"It seems he believes in my identity as the founder of the Qi Cultivation System."

"Well, that’s good; I can spare his life."

She no longer concerned herself with Meng Junzi, returning to the small shop.

By now, Elder Bai Hun of the Ruthless Sect had long fled the shop, what did it matter being chased by someone at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage outside when there were two Immortals here!

Ashy Bean shouted to the back kitchen, "Little Lotus, let’s go."

Ashy Bean called out, but receiving no response from the kitchen, she walked straight in.

During the previous meal at the diner, if Meng Junzi had extended his Immortal Sense, he would’ve found that Ashy Bean was not alone in the kitchen; there were two people.

The porridge that Meng Junzi ate was made by the other person.

A woman dressed in a sky-blue dress was wiping the stove in the kitchen, methodically cleaning various cooking utensils and placing them into the Storage Ring.

She turned her head to look at Ashy Bean, who was peering in through the lifted door curtain, sighed deeply, but did not stop her hands from working.

"Why bother fighting with him? If you don’t make a move, who would know you’re an Immortal?"

Ashy Bean went over to help Qinghe pack things up, "Seeing him reminded me of the Yingtian Immortal, just felt annoyed. If I am pursuing Transcendence, why should I suppress myself?"

Qinghe shook a small bottle used for holding salt, which was empty, "That’s why we need to move now."

Whether Ashy Bean left Meng Junzi alive or not, the small diner had been exposed. Ashy Bean wasn’t afraid of anyone other than Yun Zhi, but she still found it troublesome.

Rather than waiting for trouble to come knocking, it’s better to move somewhere else and continue the business.

After all, the Cultivation World is so vast; anywhere will do.

As they spoke, the two had already packed everything into the Storage Ring.

Actually, if Qinghe desired, she could’ve swept everything into the Storage Ring with a single gesture, but she chose to pack item by item because she felt there was a sense of ritual to it.

If the real adult were here, she would probably do the same.

The two strolled in the rain without any presence, as if invisible. Even if passersby rushed past or if the heavily guarded city gate sentinels were present, none noticed them.

"We’ve stayed in Celestial King City for so long, it’s quite good to change places," Ashy Bean initiated the conversation.

"Little Lotus, do you want to continue staying in Buddha Country or switch to another place?"

Qinghe didn’t follow the conversation and turned her head to ask, "Why do you keep me around? If you’re pursuing Transcendence, wouldn’t killing me take you a step further? There’s no need to save me for last."

Ashy Bean’s brows slightly furrowed, showing an imperceptible wrinkle. Reluctant to discuss the topic, she still said, "After I revived, it was you who were always with me. Since you can’t escape anyway, why should I be in a hurry to kill you?"

She paused, then added as if compelled by some unknown force, "If after killing everyone, I am infinitely close to Transcendence and still unable to defeat the murderer, it won’t be too late to kill you then."

Qinghe fell silent for a moment, then suddenly said.

"Watch your words. You aren’t ’revived’, you are not her, and you will never become her."

"What did you say!"

Ashy Bean flew into a rage, grabbing Qinghe by the neck. Fury blazed in her eyes, her fingers applying slight pressure, as if she could snap Qinghe’s neck at any moment.

"Don’t think I will definitely save you for last!"

Ashy Bean tore through the Spiritual Qi Shield protecting Qinghe. The rain poured down heavily, instantly soaking Qinghe.

Through the gaps in her wet hair, Qinghe looked at Ashy Bean with a derisive gaze, completely fearless, "You don’t even know your own name."

Ashy Bean looked into Qinghe’s resigned eyes, released her grip, and let Qinghe go with a cold snort.

"I will have my own name."

...

Meng Junzi was limping, supported into the Western Paradise Temple by the Meng Family’s Transcendance Tribulation Stage ancestor.

"Ouch—"

He had just sat on the bed when he touched a wound inadvertently and the pain made him stand up straight away.

How did he end up like this when he was just in Buddha Country to enjoy blessings?

Master Mingyu was greatly startled to see Meng Junzi in such a state. When had such an eminent figure come to Buddha Country, capable of beating Meng Junzi to such an extent?

"Ancestor, the investigation results of the small diner have come out," the Meng Family’s Transcendance Tribulation Stage ancestor said with utmost respect.

Although they had captured Bai Hun, Bai Hun was not the focus now; the focus was the cooking maid who claimed to be the first Immortal of Ancient Times.

"Tell me, what have you found out?"

"From the testimonies of neighbors and those living nearby, that small restaurant at the end of the alley has been there for ten years. Hardly anyone goes there to eat, and it seems that anyone who has eaten there loses their memory. They forget what the restaurant owner looks like and what they themselves had eaten."

"Memory loss?" Meng Junzi raised his eyebrow, his interest piqued. How could someone just lose their memory all of a sudden?

Was it a deliberate result of the cooking maid’s actions?

For what reason?

"Forget it, you continue the investigation of the Ruthless Sect here, I’ll go back for now."

Meng Junzi felt it necessary to consult with Old Jiang and Daoist Yun Zhi about the day’s events.

...

The Seek Dao Sect.

"Daoist Yun Zhi, that’s what happened. The founder of the Qi Cultivation System must be an ancient being beyond belief."

Yun Zhi looked at Meng Junzi with a strange gaze. The Grey Immortal spared your life.

Take on causality with a non-existent identity, so Meng Junzi won’t generate causality with the Grey Immortal?

Perhaps it’s better not to tell Meng Junzi the true identity of the Grey Immortal, lest she sets her sights on him.

With a slightly emotional tone, Yun Zhi said, "I never expected that the immortal who fought with me in the East Sea was the founder of the Qi Cultivation System. No wonder she was tough to deal with."

Meng Junzi: "..."

When you say tough to deal with, do you mean how you made her flee in a sorry state?

"Right, did you say that everyone who went to her restaurant to eat lost their memory?" Yun Zhi remembered another important point that Meng Junzi had mentioned.

"Yes, Daoist Yun Zhi, do you know what’s going on with that?"

Yun Zhi leaned back in the Emperor’s Chair, rhythmically rocking the armrest while the bells tied to her wrist jingled.

As the sound of the bells faded, Yun Zhi opened her eyes, having conceived some ideas.

"In my opinion, there are two possibilities."

"The first is that she used the power of the Dao Fruit while cooking. As a result, anyone who ate the food would lose their memory. However, you didn’t detect the power of the Dao Fruit in the gruel she served you, so the first possibility is unlikely."

"And the second possibility?"

"The second possibility is that she’s gradually approaching the Transcendent Realm. An immortal’s forgetfulness trait has amplified, automatically severing some minor causality, causing ordinary people to forget about her."

Meng Junzi drew a sharp breath. If that was the case, then this founder of the Qi Cultivation System was terrifyingly powerful, no wonder he couldn’t defeat her.

"However, these are just hypotheses, after all, I’ve never encountered such an immortal," Yun Zhi cautioned, implying her words should not be taken as the absolute truth.

The news of the battle between the two immortals quickly spread throughout the Buddha Country.

"A duel between two immortals in Celestial King City?" Lu Yang was quite surprised when he heard the news.

No, he was actually quite happy.

At last, it was proven that major events didn’t only happen where he was. He had never heard of Celestial King City before, and it absolutely had nothing to do with him.

"Which two immortals were fighting?" Lu Yang asked Meng Jingzhou, who had gathered this information.

"One of them is an ancestor of mine, the other I’m not sure about," Meng Jingzhou said.

"But it was said that while my ancestor, Cha Wuqing, was looking for the whereabouts of the Ruthless Sect, he accidentally encountered another immortal. A misunderstanding ensued, leading to the fight."

"...Your ancestor coming to the Buddha Country has nothing to do with me, right? I’m just a messenger," Lu Yang pointed out.

Meng Jingzhou patted Lu Yang on the shoulder, saying earnestly, "No, it has nothing to do with either of us."

On the fifteenth of May, the Buddha Bathing Festival.

All Kaihuang City was aflutter with excitement, homes were decorated with lights and colors, and the citizens rose early to bow before the Buddha statues in their homes.

If they could, they’d also go to Kaihuang Temple to pay respects to the Buddha and provide a meal for the monks, thus commemorating the Worldly Venerable’s birth, which illustrates the people of Kaihuang City’s devout Buddhism and their reverence for the Worldly Venerable.

Even someone like Lu Yang, who didn’t understand the Power of Incense and Fire, could feel its emergence at that moment.

Perhaps the leaderless Power of Incense and Fire in Buddha Country was so profound precisely because it had been nurtured day after day like this.

Yet there was one person who had some reservations about this.

"It’s not this Immortal’s birthday today," Fairy Eternity pouted, clearly not pleased.

Lu Yang’s heart stirred, and he asked, "Then, Fairy, when is your birthday?"

Considering how long he had known Fairy, he still didn’t know her birthday.

"The first of June."

"So what’s special about today?" Lu Yang felt there must be some significant reason for creating a festival out of nowhere; there had to be a commemoration behind it.

Fairy Eternity touched her chin and squeaked softly, thinking Little Yang’s question was particularly tricky: "The fifteenth of May, well, this Immortal has been through it so many times, who knows... Ah, no, wait, this Immortal is only sixteen years old."

Fairy Eternity looked at Lu Yang warily, hoping he hadn’t overheard her muttering to herself. freēwēbnovel.com

As a minister, Lu Yang knew all too well that even if he heard something, he should pretend he didn’t; he asked with a look of utter cluelessness: "Fairy, why are you staring at me like that?"

Fairy Eternity then relaxed and continued to reminisce.

"I remember now, today is the anniversary of my first victory over Yingtian Immortal and those four after I became a fairy!"

Lu Yang looked at the crowds splashing water in celebration of the festival, his expression becoming subtle.

Was today really worth celebrating?

The streets of Kaihuang City were bustling, more crowded than ever before in the city’s history, surpassing the excitement of any previous Buddha Bathing Festival.

Even Master Duanchen was overjoyed; he knew of the influence of Lu Yang and his companion, but he hadn’t expected it to be so great, several times higher than the previous record, to the point where even the monks maintaining order were insufficient, and manpower was somewhat stretched thin.

As they passed by, Lu Yang and his partner glanced at the noisy arena, which was surrounded by crowds of people.

On the stage, Qi Refinement, Foundation Establishment, and Gold Core Period Cultivators showcased their Divine Abilities, all vying for a place in the preliminary round.

As judges, Lu Yang and his companion obviously couldn’t comment on each and every match—that would be devaluing themselves too much.

Only when the cultivators made their way through the preliminaries, stood out from the crowd, and entered the top eight would Lu Yang and his companion appear as judges to comment.

Therefore, every cultivator, regardless of the prizes, wanted to find a way to squeeze into the top eight to earn the feedback of the two judges.

If either of them praised someone even a bit, it could make that person famous.

"The levels are all quite average," Lu Yang observed briefly; they were all mid-level in their respective ranks, the good ones were just above the midpoint, hardly able to challenge those of a higher level.

"Make do with it. You think this is our Sect, where Geniuses are a dime a dozen."

Suddenly, the crowd started to stir, and someone pointed at a Gold Core Cultivator stepping onto the stage, visibly astonished: "Look, that’s Huo Ying; it’s said he completed the Vermilion Bird Trial at Vermilion Bird Temple and rose to the ninety-ninth place on the Earth Rankings!"

"Why would he come here?"

Lu Yang looked puzzled and turned to Meng Jingzhou, "What the heck is the Earth Ranking?"

Meng Jingzhou shook his head as well, "I’ve never heard of it."

Lu Yang patted the shoulder of a spectator shouting the loudest on the outer edge, figuring he would know.

"Excuse me, could you tell me what this Earth Ranking is?"

The man turned around, surprised at Lu Yang’s question, "You don’t know what the Earth Ranking is?"

"Um, we’re cultivators from Great Xia, here in Buddha Country to compete," Lu Yang honestly explained.

"No wonder you don’t know. Our Buddha Country’s Western Paradise Temple initiated the ranking to inspire cultivators, giving our Buddha Country cultivators their own ranking."

"There are three lists in total, People’s List for the Foundation Establishment Stage, Earth Ranking for the Golden Core Stage, and Heaven Ranking for the Nascent Soul Stage, each with a hundred slots."

"See that Huo Ying on stage? He’s ranked ninety-ninth on the Earth Ranking of the geniuses, the ninety-ninth among Golden Core Stage cultivators. It’s said that even the average Nascent Soul Early Stage cultivator is no match for him. Although there’s no record of his battles yet, everyone says his strength is on par with that of veteran Nascent Soul Early Stage cultivators!"

The man became increasingly excited as he spoke, as if Huo Ying were some kind of big shot.

"Who would’ve thought he would participate in Kaihuang City’s Buddha Bathing Festival? With him here, I’m afraid the other cultivators won’t stand a chance!"

Lu Yang suddenly realized why this Huo Ying looked somewhat distinguished — to rank among the geniuses of Buddha Country’s Golden Core Stage was to be on par with Lady Whitebone herself.

"Why don’t they continue the rankings above the Heaven List? I wanted to see where I could rank myself," Meng Jingzhou said regretfully shaking his head. He had come to Buddha Country too late; had he known about the rankings, he would’ve come during his Nascent Soul Stage.

Suddenly, the crowd cheered again, louder and more excited than before.

"It’s Fang Wudi, ranked ninety-fifth on the Earth Ranking, he’s here too!"

"What, the Fang Wudi who acquired the supreme technique from the Hengsha Secret Realm?"

"Even he’s come!"

"A battle between dragons and tigers!"

Two great Earth Ranking cultivators clashing — such a rare fight!

"Fang Wudi, I didn’t expect you’d come," Huo Ying said, his expression serious, as if facing a great enemy. He had never sparred with Fang Wudi but had heard many stories about him. The one ranked above him had valid reasons for it.

"I heard you’re a Venerate Exalted Body, born with a Golden Dragon coiling into your body and becoming your birthmark.

Then at noon, you absorbed pure Yang energy, beginning Qi Refinement, achieved Foundation Establishment in a hundred days, condensed your Golden Core in the Hengsha Secret Realm, and with immense Body Refinement turned your body as tough as iron and copper bones — taking the Body Refinement path almost to the extreme!"

"Just passing by, thought I’d try my luck," said Fang Wudi as he took out an iron staff made of refined steel from his Storage Ring, which had claimed the lives of countless desperate souls.

"You’re not too shabby either, Huo Ying.

I’ve heard your mother is the Holy Daughter of the Profound Mystery Land, and that you were tempered with great medicine before birth, born holding a strand of innate purple Qi, then you fought against wolf thieves and flying corpses, traversed three thousand miles of the desert, escorted the sacred object to fight Wudi, burst into rage for your beloved, left the Holy Land with no regrets — you’re admirable..."

The two men locked eyes, a fight ready to erupt at any moment!

The audience was boiling with excitement, not expecting to witness such a battle at the start of the Buddha Bathing Festival!

Lu Yang watched the fight between Huo Ying and Fang Wudi closely, observing them being evenly matched, and couldn’t help but marvel at the difficulty of imagining the three people ranked between them.

"Buddha Country really does have its experts, ah, such a small gap and yet they managed to come up with a ranking."

Meng Jingzhou watched for a long time without seeing anything outstanding about the two.

"No, these two have been bragging about each other for half the day, is this all they’ve got? Back in my Golden Core Stage, I could’ve taken on both of them at once."

Meng Jingzhou listened as the two people introduced each other; one’s background was more astonishing than the other’s, whether it was reaching the pinnacle of Body Refinement or having a mother who was a Holy Daughter of the sacred grounds.

Once they crossed hands, he found that their combat strength was indeed mediocre. Not to mention anything else, the Body Refinement Realm that he himself had mastered during the Golden Core Stage was much stronger than Fang Wudi’s.

Back then, he had refined his body from his hair to his shadow, not a single flaw to be found.

In contrast, Fang Wudi’s Body Refinement Realm was full of holes and totally uninspired.

"What’s the matter; do you want to go up there and practice with them?" Lu Yang glanced at Meng Jingzhou, who was itching to try.

"That wouldn’t be appropriate," Meng Jingzhou waved his hand, saying with reserved pride, "After all, I’m now considered a Great Power of Cultivation, a giant of the Righteous Path. It would be beneath me to go on stage and fight with the younger generation."

"...But these two seem to be only three years younger than you."

"They’re still the younger generation. You see, when we Immortal practitioners get angry, we often say ’How dare you, young one.’ We never say ’How dare you, peer.’ This shows that calling them ’young one’ carries more weight."

Lu Yang nodded, agreeing that Old Meng had a point.

Continuing to watch the Golden Core Stage fights here was not very interesting, so the two decided to come back when the monks from Kaihuang Temple informed them of the selection results for the top eight.

"Eh, it’s Master Lu, Master Meng." freēnovelkiss.com

Only the two of them had seen what they looked like after disguising themselves.

Tang Qiaoqiao and Cui Que’er held candied haw in their hands, cherishing them. The candied haw were lifelike portraits of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

The skill was honed by the candy sculptor overnight to meet the demand, and the effect was surprisingly good.

Tang Qiaoqiao sighed; she’d been looking forward to spending the festival with her brother, but now it seemed unlikely.

After receiving a drop of Lu Yang’s blood as a blessing, Tang Qiaoqiao’s and Cui Que’er’s bodies had already transformed, becoming much stronger than even ordinary warriors.

Lu Yang thought to himself that there was really no need for that last part; the Worldly Venerable can’t bless me at all.

"Of course, of course."

As the two men wandered along the street, many people were licking sugar paintings bearing their likenesses, treating the images in a way that made both men feel quite odd.

Suddenly, a man in a black cloak appeared in front of them, laughing eerily with a very strange voice.

He turned around, holding a pitch-black needle, his eyes manic and he burst into frenzied laughter, leaving Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou utterly bewildered.

"The chaos of Kaihuang City begins with you two. If you’re looking for someone to blame, it’s just your bad luck!"

With that, the man in the black cloak thrust the needle toward Meng Jingzhou’s arm with force!

Crack—

The needle snapped into two pieces upon striking Meng Jingzhou’s arm.

The scene fell silent.

The man in the black cloak glanced at the broken needle, then at Meng Jingzhou, and turned to flee.

Meng Jingzhou launched a hand strike that sent the man in the black cloak tumbling, his body tilting as he fell to the ground.

"What on earth is this?" Meng Jingzhou said, holding half of the needle, still not understanding the situation.

"Fairy, can you make out what this is?"

"Let the Immortal take a look, hmm, this needle’s been poisoned, and the components are quite complex. It seems like the person pricked will become delirious and irrational, biting anyone on sight, and anyone bitten will exhibit the same symptoms."

Lu Yang: "..."

This symptom—why does it sound so familiar? Wait, isn’t this just like a zombie?

Upon learning about the needle’s effects, Lu Yang no longer held back. He dragged the man in the black cloak into an alley to perform a Soul Search, to understand the full story.

It turned out the Abbot of another monastery was envious of the prosperity of Kaihuang City and wanted to create chaos by having someone on the street randomly prick a few unlucky individuals to become the sources of contagion.

Meng Jingzhou happened to be the first unlucky one.

"Enough, let’s report this to Master Duanchen and let him handle it," Lu Yang said, stretching. Since it was an issue targeting Kaihuang City, naturally, they should notify Master Duanchen. They were not responsible for what followed.

"It seems that the heavens are on our side, today is indeed a good day for doing good deeds," Meng Jingzhou said gleefully, eliciting a nod from Lu Yang in agreement. This act was the same as saving all the citizens of the city, a great merit indeed.

On their way back to Kaihuang Temple, they encountered a Lascivious Monk practicing the Joyous Buddha, attempting to kidnap a common girl to be his twenty-sixth concubine; a cultivator desperate for self-detonation as his lifespan neared the end; a cultivator about to hold an unrestricted gathering after learning a Hypnosis Technique; an Insect Cultivator nearly causing an insect calamity after being counterattacked by the Insect King; an evil practitioner about to unleash a plague and wreak havoc among the people; a cultivator who had captured the young of the Beast King, risking the onset of a beast tide...

Before long, there was a rope in Lu Yang’s hand, and behind him was a line of cultivators, all obediently following Lu Yang.

Master Duanchen sat at the entrance of the temple, watching the endless stream of pilgrims with a smile on his face, feeling more and more content that inviting Lu Yang and his companion to Kaihuang City had been the right decision.

He believed that after the Buddha Bathing Festival, he would take a big step towards his ambitious goal.

"Benefactors, how come you are back?" Master Duanchen, surprised to hear of their return, came out to greet them.

Then he saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou leading several people.

"Who are these people?"

Lu Yang handed the rope to Master Duanchen with an expressionless face and said, "The results of doing good deeds."

"Also, the public security in your Kaihuang City is really too poor."

"Ah?" Master Duanchen was confused, "Benefactor Lu, is your way of accumulating good deeds by bringing a group of people back with you?"

"This one practices the Joyful Zen."

"This one wants to commit suicide."

"This one knows the Hypnosis Technique..."

Lu Yang introduced each person’s background one by one, each worthy of mention. Just capturing them was no easy task, not something that could be summed up in a sentence or two.

When he got to the last one, Lu Yang gravely said, "Luckily, Old Meng and I felt that something significant would happen at the festival and were restless. We kept an eye on unusual activities in the city, and look, we found them all."

Listening, Master Duanchen broke out in a cold sweat. These people were all significant threats. If Benefactor Lu and Benefactor Meng had missed even one person, this Buddha Bathing Festival would have been doomed.

But it wasn’t his fault for the lack of preparation; these troublesome cultivators all acted covertly, and even increasing patrols wouldn’t have uncovered them.

"I wonder how you two benefactors managed to find these people, could you possibly teach me a technique or two?"

Lu Yang waved his hand modestly, "There’s no special technique, it’s just the protection of the Worldly Venerable."

Master Duanchen was moved by these words; indeed, that was the only possibility. Otherwise, even if they both had been using Spiritual Sense non-stop, it was impossible to find everyone.

"It seems both benefactors are individuals of profound fortune."

"Master, you are weary from dealing with these people, and I estimate the top eight are about to be chosen; it’s time for Old Meng and me to go to the scene," Lu Yang calculated the time and said.

Initially, after they captured the person releasing the zombie poison, they had quite a lot of time to play, but who could have expected there was a whole bunch of people waiting to be caught? After capturing them all and sending them back to Kaihuang Temple, the time was almost up.

"Indeed."

The moment Lu Yang stepped out of the temple gate, his vision darkened, and when he regained his sight, he was already near the arena.
