These were obtained from the Three-eyed Ghost Monk, most of which were in Meng Jingzhou’s possession!

Elder Wu Shui was stunned for a moment, almost thinking Meng Jingzhou was one of their own from the Ruthless Sect.

He quickly came back to his senses, the power of the Pure Yang Dharma Aspect was advancing, and his own Dharma Aspect was about to collapse!

Meng Jingzhou felt an unprecedentedly good condition, a clear mind state, now he could wholeheartedly engage in the battle without worrying about his body!

"Kill."

As the four were entangled in the melee, an even more tyrannical pressure enveloped Kaihuang City, interrupting their fight.

"It seems that the young ones are quite capable these days, even challenging those in the Body Integration Realm."

An ancient figure appeared, not smiling genuinely, his gaze occasionally drifting toward Lu Yang.

"Are you Ye Zijin’s Junior Brother?"

"Vice Sect Hierarch!" Bai Liting and Wu Shui stopped attacking and flew to the side of the aged figure, bowing respectfully.

The Vice Sect Hierarch of the Ruthless Sect!

"The time is about right. It’s time to take something from Buddha Country when we leave, to give both Buddha Country and Great Xia a long-lasting lesson. This Kaihuang City should go as well."

The elderly figure spoke indifferently, and Kaihuang City trembled continuously, lifting off the ground and flying into the sky.

Then, darkness fell before Lu Yang’s eyes.

"Old Lu, do you want to see how their fight is going?" Meng Jingzhou pointed at the arena and said.

"Back again."

Lu Yang took a deep breath in and out, calming his mind state.

Just moments ago, he was fighting for his life, but in the blink of an eye, time had flowed backward, restoring the peaceful days. The contrast was so great that it gave Lu Yang a feeling as if he was in a different world.

At least, it was peace on the surface.

Based on the timeline, the two elders from the Ruthless Sect should have already poisoned the canal by now, and the water currently being splashed all over the streets contained the Forgetfulness Poison, though it hadn’t fully evaporated yet.

For instance, the agitation of the Insect King, an Insect Cultivator, was due to the absorption of the Forgetfulness Poison.

It was possible that some children had already been poisoned, but because children had little influence, no one had noticed.

"Fairy, are those two elders and the Vice Sect Hierarch still in Kaihuang City?"

Fairy Eternity extended her Spiritual Sense to sense and responded, "They’re not here."

Lu Yang nodded, knowing this result was within his expectations. If those two Ruthless Sect elders had been in Kaihuang City, they wouldn’t have allowed him and Old Meng to stage a play throughout the city and only reveal themselves after the show was over.

Right now, they should be elsewhere.

A knowing smile tugged at the corner of Lu Yang’s mouth.

It took a struggle to handle two elders, and when that was done, the Vice Sect Hierarch stepped in, proud of your numbers, huh?

"Old Meng, stop watching the competition for now. There are several good deeds awaiting your action right now," Lu Yang said.

"What good deeds?" Meng Jingzhou was puzzled by Lu Yang’s sudden statement.

"Go to Yellowstone Street now, on that street, there’s someone in a black cloak, laughing strangely and holding silver needles; catch him. Then turn a corner to the entrance of the civilian restaurant, there’s a fat monk in fancy clothing... and after passing through another street, you’ll meet an old man trying to self-detonate..."

Meng Jingzhou listened to Lu Yang’s detailed information, which didn’t seem deceitful.

"What about you, what will you do?"

"I’m going to call for help," Lu Yang said, before weaving through the crowd and returning to his guest room in Kaihuang Temple, collapsing into sleep.

...

Seek Dao Sect, Task Hall, Soul Lamp Chamber.

Lu Yang’s Soul Lamp flickered on and off, prompting Gu Junye to hastily call for Dai Bufan.

Dai Bufan studied the pattern of the Soul Lamp’s flickering and deciphered the message Lu Yang was sending.

"Should we ask Vast Sea Ancestral Master to open a passage from Kaihuang City back to the Sect, so Junior Brother Lu can return for a while?"

...

Across the vast desert, a few people riding camels were especially conspicuous against the sands.

"No!" Tang Chuanwu suddenly woke up, his eyes filled with panic.

"Tang boy, what’s wrong?" The middle-aged man with a beard noticed Tang Chuanwu’s distress and signaled for the caravan to halt.

"Back again." Tang Chuanwu muttered to himself, as if awakening from a dream, drenched in sweat. How many times had he experienced this Reincarnation, the sixth or the seventh?

The shock from the end of the last cycle was tremendous, and right now, his mind was a total mess; he needed to sort out the sequence of events.

They were all from a medicine shop in Kaihuang City, currently short on supplies and en route to Lotus City to procure medicinal materials.

On their way to Lotus City, they encountered an exceptionally rare pack of Sand Wolves. These Sand Wolves were cunning and extremely dangerous, with the Wolf King being a being at the Consummation of Qi Refinement level.

They had martial arts skills on their travels, and even Tang Chuanwu’s combat strength was the highest among them all.

But even so, facing the premeditated attack of the Wolf King, they couldn’t escape their fate.

```

Tang Chuanwu used five reincarnations to match wits and bravery against the Wolf King, yet he still couldn’t defeat the Wolf King, and the entire team was on the verge of being slaughtered by the wolves.

During the fifth reincarnation, despite his meticulous planning, the Wolf King fell into a trap he had set, only for it to breakthrough to the terrifying Foundation Establishment Stage at the very last moment, turning all his plans into a joke.

Tang Chuanwu was nearly driven insane; the Wolf King was simply not an opponent he could deal with. He had encountered cultivators as opponents before, but that was in the city where he could stir various conflicts and maneuver through them.

But this was the desert, where there was neither village ahead nor shop behind, and he couldn’t find anyone to match the Wolf King!

On the sixth reincarnation, no longer able to bear this torment, he stopped trying to save his team and rode back to Kaihuang City alone on a camel to seek help; perhaps, he could still save one or two people this way.

But when he returned to Kaihuang City, what greeted him was a city full of heartless people; he couldn’t find any help at all, and the two masters were still dealing with two elders from the Ruthless Sect.

In desperation, he returned home to see how his sister was doing.

It was already noon by then, and Cui Que’er had finished distributing porridge and had not yet left the slums. An unknown Gold Core Period Cultivator had taken a fancy to Cui Que’er’s beauty and kidnapped her in the chaos, despite his shouts and struggles being futile.

He staggered back home only to find his sister looking at him expressionlessly, as if looking at a stranger, a look that tore at his heart.

Then, the Vice Sect Hierarch of the Ruthless Sect made a move, intending to relocate the entire Kaihuang City.

Finally, unable to bear the torment any longer, he committed suicide and arrived at the seventh reincarnation.

Tang Chuanwu was filled with despair; he knew that the Wolf King was waiting in ambush, a Gold Core Period Cultivator had kidnapped Cui Que’er in Kaihuang City, and there was a Demon Path giant planning to move the entire city.

None was an opponent he could handle!

What should he do? What was he supposed to do?

"Kid Tang?" A middle-aged man with a beard muttered to himself, wondering what was wrong with the usually clever Tang Chuanwu today.

Tang Chuanwu had thought that upon his previous return to Kaihuang City, the problem could have been easily resolved, but the last reincarnation taught him that Kaihuang City was an even more dangerous place than the desert! freewebnσvel.cøm

Even if he could go back in time, what use was it? He couldn’t save anyone; he could only save himself!

Moments of the last reincarnation kept flooding his mind—the team mauled by wolves, Cui Que’er being kidnapped, his sister’s indifferent expression, Kaihuang City flying away...

"Ah—" Overwhelmed by chaos, Tang Chuanwu screamed to the sky, completely unable to think of a solution.

Suddenly, a sentence Master Lu had told him after annihilating the Skull Divine Sect flashed in his mind.

"We will be staying at Kaihuang Temple for a while longer; if you encounter any trouble, feel free to come find me."

...

As the spatial passage closed, Lu Yang, holding the Green Peak Sword, returned to his room in Kaihuang Temple.

He put away the Green Peak Sword, left Kaihuang Temple, and prepared to meet up with Old Meng.

A shadow rode swiftly on a camel through the streets.

Tang Chuanwu gazed eagerly at Lu Yang, who stood somewhat dazed at the temple’s entrance, and felt as if a weight had been lifted. He tumbled down from the camel with a clatter.

With the experience of six reincarnations behind him, bypassing the Wolf King, he sprinted all the way, finally finding Lu Yang—his only lifeline—before the Forgetfulness Poison fully erupted.

Lu Yang, quick to react, stepped forward to catch Tang Chuanwu, who nearly fell to the ground.

With a look of despair, Tang Chuanwu said, "Master Lu, this city is in danger!"

"The Ruthless Sect’s people will come to Kaihuang City, everyone will become heartless, and I don’t know how they do it, but it must be the work of the Ruthless Sect. The first two people who appear, you can handle, but the last one that appears, neither you nor Master Meng can handle."

"You might not believe me, Master, but everything I am saying is true, it’s all true!"

The more Tang Chuanwu spoke, the more agitated he became, until his emotions collapsed. He started speaking incoherently and couldn’t help but burst into tears. He really didn’t know what to do, whether Master Lu would believe him, or if there was a solution...

"I believe you."

```

"What exactly are you saying, Master?" Tang Chuanwu thought he must be hallucinating, as the words he spoke were illogical and incoherent. How could Master Lu possibly believe him?

Lu Yang looked into Tang Chuanwu’s eyes and repeated himself seriously.

"I believe."

Tang Chuanwu’s lips trembled, unsure whether he was laughing or crying: "You believe me, someone really believes me, I wasn’t lying..."

The opportunity he discovered to possess the Time Retrospection ability stemmed from an attack targeting his sister. In the second reincarnation, he excitedly held his sister back, telling her you are in danger if you go out, you will be killed, you can’t go out.

However, what he got in return was his sister’s look of astonishment.

His sister didn’t believe him and died in the second reincarnation.

After that, he tried to save others with his Time Retrospection ability, warning them of future dangers, advising them not to take certain actions. Even when the future events confirmed his words, the result was only increased distrust.

In subsequent reincarnations, he calmed down and learned to save people using the differences in information and lies.

This time, he had an emotional breakdown and had no choice but to reveal the truth to Lu Yang. He thought Master Lu, like everyone else, wouldn’t believe him at all, yet Master Lu believed him.

Finally, someone believed him.

The clue about the Time Dao Fruit user has finally been found.

"Sit down, don’t rush, take your time to talk. What exactly happened today, and how did you know about it?"

Lu Yang quietly channeled spiritual essence into Tang Chuanwu to stabilize his emotions.

He could feel Tang Chuanwu’s pulse racing, the frequency terribly high, reaching the limit of what a mortal can withstand, indicating how agitated he had been.

Or perhaps how desperate.

Of course, Lu Yang would believe him; Tang Chuanwu appearing before him at this particular time point was evidence itself.

At this time, Tang Chuanwu should have been far away in Lotus City and not supposed to be here.

His presence here could only mean one thing—he knew what the future would bring.

The incoherent words that followed from Tang Chuanwu further confirmed Lu Yang’s suspicions.

With Lu Yang’s reassurance, Tang Chuanwu gradually calmed down.

"Master Lu, a major catastrophe is about to happen in the city. Everyone will become extremely indifferent. I don’t know what’s going on, but it must be related to the Ruthless Sect," he said.

"And the Skull Divine Sect’s Master, I don’t know how, but he’s resurrected and has become the White Skeleton Champion. The White Skeleton Champion is no match for you."

"Later on, two Elders and the Vice Sect Hierarch of the Ruthless Sect showed up. That Vice Sect Hierarch is incredibly powerful; he even wanted to move Kaihuang City. Neither you nor Master Meng could match him."

"Also, Queer... a Golden Core cultivator will abduct her."

Lu Yang quietly listened to Tang Chuanwu’s description, then extended two fingers and looked into Tang Chuanwu’s eyes.

"I only have two questions. First, how did you come to know all of this?"

"I can..." Tang Chuanwu began to speak, wanted to say Time Retrospection, but then suddenly remembered that once he said it, time would rewind again.

"Is it Time Retrospection?" Lu Yang asked calmly.

The chair clattered to the ground as Tang Chuanwu abruptly stood up, looking incredulously at Master Lu.

Tang Chuanwu dared not confirm nor deny, worried that either answer might trigger the Time Retrospection.

"Immortal Fairy, what’s going on here? If Tang Chuanwu can perform Time Retrospection, why isn’t the Time Dao Fruit with him?"

Immortal Fairy Eternity had clearly checked; there was no Time Dao Fruit on Tang Chuanwu.

Inside the Spiritual Space, Immortal Fairy Eternity sat cross-legged on the Lotus Platform, idly swinging a little foot back and forth.

"Hmm~ Since he doesn’t have the Time Dao Fruit, there’s another possibility. The user of the Time Dao Fruit might have applied its power to him."

"What do you mean?"

"You remember what Immortal I told you, don’t you? If I wish, I can use the Eternity Dao Fruit to make everyone in the world immortal."

Lu Yang recalled, "You also said that the Dao Fruit itself represents a rule. Whether you apply that rule to yourself or to everyone else is entirely up to you."

Immortal Fairy Eternity was pleased that Lu Yang remembered her words: "The Time Dao Fruit works the same way. Its user can apply the ’Time Retrospection’ rule to this Tang fellow."

"So it’s like that," Lu Yang was astonished, he had only heard the Immortal talk about it casually and hadn’t given it much thought before. Now, seeing Tang Chuanwu possess such a heaven-defying ability, he realized Immortals indeed were extraordinary beings.

"It seems like my guess was correct; you do have the ability for Time Retrospection."

Seeing Tang Chuanwu still hesitant, Lu Yang nodded, "It seems you’re not unwilling to admit it, but rather you can’t say it out loud."

"Will you die, or will time rewind... Never mind, that’s not important."

"Second question, before the Ruthless Sect appeared, you went through five reincarnations. Did anything happen to you that requires my help?"

Tang Chuanwu’s eyes widened in shock. Master Lu actually retained memories from his previous reincarnations!

The reason he hadn’t mentioned the sand wolf attack was that he felt such an incident couldn’t be changed. After seeing Master Lu, all his previous thoughts were overturned.

"Yes, our team was attacked by sand wolves on the way to Lotus City, and only I survived and escaped!"

"I see." Lu Yang finally understood why he was caught in the cycle of reincarnation today.

He crossed his arms and propped up his head, "Then let me ask you, are you willing to save them?"

"I am willing!"

Lu Yang stood up and caressed the Green Peak Sword, it seemed this reincarnation had people coming over for nothing.

"Then you initiate time retrospection, and I will go rescue your team."

As Lu Yang looked on in astonishment, Tang Chuanwu pulled out the dagger from his waist and stabbed directly into his chest without any hesitation.

...

Tang Chuanwu suddenly awoke to find himself riding a camel, the conversation with Master Lu felt like a dream.

"Little Tang, what’s wrong?" The medicine shop owner noticed something odd with Tang Chuanwu and signaled for the caravan to stop.

"Owner, the sand wolves have marked us," Tang Chuanwu calmly took out a string of Buddha Beads from his chest, snapping it with two fingers as he extracted it.

"I had the fortune of encountering Master Duanchen welcoming guests. These Buddha Beads were given to me by Master Duanchen, and they will alert me when danger is near."

"What?!" Seeing Tang Chuanwu’s serious manner, the medicine shop owner did not doubt him.

Facing a pack of sand wolves would mean almost certain death for a caravan like theirs.

"Don’t panic, let’s continue moving forward and not let the sand wolves notice anything unusual," Tang Chuanwu, experienced in dealing with sand wolves, gave instructions. "We’ll hold off the pack. Someone will come to save us."

If they showed a defensive stance now, the sand wolves would notice their failed ambush and attack directly. Continuing forward might delay their assault.

"Okay, okay." The medicine shop owner was flustered and had no choice but to follow his lead.

The camel caravan slowly moved on.

"It’s the sand wolves!" Suddenly, someone with sharp eyes shouted, and the team immediately fell into chaos.

Sand wolves, with only their nostrils showing as they looked up from being buried in the sand, suddenly burst out of the desert and pounced on the caravan.

"Prepare yourselves! Don’t panic!" The medicine shop owner drew his sword to defend.

Tang Chuanwu, riding a camel and heading straight for the Wolf King, had his physique greatly enhanced by a drop of Lu Yang’s blood, which strengthened his tendons and bones. Coupled with the secret practice of Long Arm Boxing, his combat capabilities were far superior to the medicine shop owner.

Even with Tang Chuanwu holding off the Wolf King, the rest of the people quickly found themselves in a standstill.

Not that Tang Chuanwu was faring any better. He was, after all, just a mortal. How could he be a match for the Wolf King, with its Cultivation of Qi Consummation?

"Tang boy, where is this savior you mentioned!" the medicine shop owner, running out of strength, shouted loudly. At this rate, none of them would be able to escape.

Hearing the owner’s question, Tang Chuanwu’s expression became vacant for a moment.

Why hadn’t Master Lu arrived yet? Was it because they were too far from Kaihuang City? Or was the last reincarnation just a hopeless dream? Would anybody really believe him?

Seeing his opportunity, the Wolf King roared and lunged at Tang Chuanwu.

"Tang boy, watch out!"

Snapped back to reality, Tang Chuanwu quickly raised his defenses, but it was too late. The Wolf King bit his knife, knocking him off the camel.

A man and a wolf wrestled in the sand. During the struggle, Tang Chuanwu’s strength began to wane.

Suddenly, a surge of Sword Qi pierced the Wolf King’s head, with the sword tip stopping mere inches from Tang Chuanwu.

Swish, swish, swish—

The person was yet to arrive, but his sword was already at work.

Sword Qi fell like rain over the desert, and the pack of sand wolves was impaled by each strike, killed in an instant. In just a moment, the entire wolf pack was decimated.

The sword-wielding Immortal flew in with the sun behind him. Amidst the shocked gaze of onlookers, he landed and pulled Tang Chuanwu to his feet.

"I’m here."

"It’s Sword Immortal Lu!" Initially, the medicine shop owner and the others were astonished to be suddenly saved by the sword qi.

But after they got a clear look at Lu Yang’s appearance, their shock turned into wild joy.

"It was Sword Immortal Lu who saved us!"

"What, still not fully awake?" Lu Yang looked at Tang Chuanwu with a dazed expression, teasing him with a smile.

"I’m awake, I’m awake." Tang Chuanwu finally convinced himself that the events from the last reincarnation weren’t an illusion. They were real, and besides himself, someone else also had memories from the reincarnation and was on his side.

Lu Yang picked up the Sand Wolf King with a pierced skull and examined it carefully. He remembered that on the way to Kaihuang City, he casually dealt with a pack of Sand Wolves and a Sand Wolf King. How could another one appear?

"I see now, wolf packs have a sense of territory. Since Old Meng and I killed the last batch of Sand Wolves, naturally another pack would migrate here."

Two groups of Sand Wolves dying near Kaihuang City should mean that, for the time being, no packs would dare to take over here.

"However, I really didn’t expect your time reversal to be triggered by death." Lu Yang was forced to endure hundreds of reincarnations, which meant Tang Chuanwu had to experience death hundreds of times, whether voluntarily or not.

"Fairy, if death can serve as a condition for time retrospection, then how was Time Immortal assassinated in the past?"

"That I don’t know. What powers a Causality Dao Fruit possesses is unknown to all. It could have been a temporary separation between Time Immortal and the Time Dao Fruit, or perhaps a reverse causality, anchoring the result of ’Time Immortal’s demise’?"

Returning to reality, Lu Yang pulled out several wooden swords and asked the caravan.

"Okay, then. Be safe on your way back." Lu Yang handed the wooden swords to the medicine shop owner, then pulled Tang Chuanwu onto the Sword Washing Pool and headed straight for Kaihuang City.

The two landed at the entrance of Kaihuang City, and Lu Yang put away the Sword Washing Pool: "You said before that a Gold Core Period Cultivator took a fancy to Cui Que’er and wanted to kidnap her?"

"Yes."

"That’s him!"

"Fang Wudi?" Lu Yang raised an eyebrow, surprised to find out that the Gold Core Period Cultivator Tang Chuanwu mentioned was none other than Fang Wudi, ranked ninety-fifth on the land ranking.

If there were no surprises in this competition, he would be the champion.

Could it be that he took a liking to Cui Que’er when Qiaoqiao and Queer passed the arena?

"He probably took interest in Queer’s Profound Yin Body," said Immortal Fairy. "This Fang has some kind of innate Venerate body, which is actually a lesser body constitution similar to the Pure Yang Constitution.

Such constitutions either end like the Meng Family Kid, walking a dark path but achieving a respectable outcome, or they utilize Yin and Yang balancing methods to suppress the Yang Qi in the body, which leads to an average future."

The Profound Yin Body, born on a Yin year, Yin month, and Yin day, counted as a special physique. Lu Yang had encountered a Foundation Establishment Stage Cultivator with this constitution during the celebrations in Qingzhou. The cultivator’s practice was not slow, lagging behind Lu Yang by only one major realm.

Lu Yang had always regarded Cui Que’er as an ordinary person, not realizing she had this kind of constitution.

"Fang Wudi."

Fang Wudi, shocked, found that his prideful golden core was like a stone ox sinking into the sea, utterly unusable, and what he called the golden core’s oppressive force couldn’t even leave his body.

The last time in the cycle of reincarnation, Fang Wudi, who couldn’t be harmed in the least by any of Tang Chuanwu’s myriad tactics, was easily subdued by Lu Yang, extinguished as effortlessly as one would crush an ant.

But it didn’t matter; Lu Yang had a more suitable candidate in mind.

Calculating the time before he set out, Lu Yang had informed Old Meng about the troubles within Kaihuang City, and by now Old Meng should have caught everyone and taken them back to Kaihuang Temple; they had agreed to meet at the temple gate.

True to expectations, Lu Yang arrived at the temple gate with Tang Chuanwu and Fang Wudi to see Meng Jingzhou just coming out.

"Back so soon? What did you go off to do in such a hurry?"

This cycle had just begun, and before the tournament where Fang Wudi was to appear had started, Lu Yang had urged Meng Jingzhou to quickly handle the trouble, hence Meng Jingzhou did not recognize Fang Wudi.

However, upon catching Fang Wudi, Meng Jingzhou could feel that he had a special constitution.

"His name is Fang Wudi, and he might be the first-place winner of this competition. He possesses an innate Venerate body, just like your Single Body Spiritual Root, both of which are of the Yang constitution. To balance Yin and Yang, he has probably coerced quite a few people."

"I need to see Elder Brother Dai; I’ll see you later."

Lu Yang took Tang Chuanwu inside the guest room of Kaihuang Temple and asked him to stay there quietly.

Then Tang Chuanwu saw Lu Yang lie on the bed, suddenly losing all signs of life, and then just as suddenly, he came back to life. Soon after, a spatial gate opened, and Lu Yang stepped through it, disappearing. A while later, the spatial gate opened again, and Lu Yang returned, holding the Green Peak Sword, his spirit bright and fresh.

Just like the sixth cycle, after the Forgetfulness Poison outbreak, Lu Yang informed Master Duanchen to take charge, and he and Old Meng acted in full view of the public, as their Bodhi clones self-destructed, leaving the citizens holding their breath.

Two figures ascended to the sky, looking down at Lu Yang and his accomplice with indifference.

"The Meng Family uprooted all of our arrangements in Buddha Country, making it impossible for us to stay. Before we leave, wouldn’t it seem like the Ruthless Sect is too weak if we don’t do something?"

Lu Yang watched the two with great interest, "Oh, from what you two are saying, it’s not only about meddling with the city’s people; you also want to deal with both of us?"

"The two of you exposed our sect’s movements, making you the culprits. You don’t run back to Great Xia, instead, you brazenly continue to stay in Buddha Country; you really don’t know the meaning of death."

Lu Yang watched the two Ruthless Sect Elders with a mocking smile, "You two are at the Mid Integration Stage, but Old Meng and I are only at the Mid-stage of Transforming Spirit; how could we possibly be your match?"

"However, it’s quite a coincidence that we happen to have someone here who is qualified to be your match."

Lu Yang raised the Green Peak Sword, and a man wearing a deep blue robe stepped out from the small world of the Green Peak Sword.

"Elder Brother Dai, you must make a decision for the two of us brothers; it was the Ruthless Sect who came looking for us first."

Dai Bufan glanced at Lu Yang, who stood honestly behind.

People from the Ruthless Sect found you first?

So how did you know the Ruthless Sect would come, and even knew to go back to the Sect to call for help?

Dai Bufan moved his body, his bones making creaking sounds. He had been in charge of the Task Hall for years, rarely needing to lift a finger, but that did not mean he had grown weak.

He had taken over the Task Hall from the Grand Elder early on, not only because the Grand Elder was lazy; the most important reason was his strength was sufficient for great responsibilities!

Among his peers, except for Yun Zhi, he had never lost to anyone!

"It’s rare to encounter the Ruthless Sect," Dai Bufan felt somewhat nostalgic. Over the years, the members of the Ruthless Sect he had seen were souls barely clinging to life; a lively Ruthless Sect Elder like this was a first.

"Sky Change!"

Dai Bufan swiftly raised his hand towards the sky, and instantly dark clouds gathered, bringing a torrential rain that had not been seen in Kaihuang City for five hundred years, instantly cooling the city and the surrounding desert.

He was a Water Spirit Root; this was his home field.

Everywhere, the whole world seemed to become a realm of water. The citizens of Kaihuang City, who had lived so long, were seeing this version of Kaihuang City for the first time.

"Rivers in Reverse!"

The rainwater flowed through the street openings like thousands of streams, which, as if alive, turned into little flood dragons attacking the two Elders.

"Black Tortoise Shell!"

"White Bone Flying Boat!"

Elders Bai Li Ting and Wu Shui had not expected Dai Bufan to cast his spells so quickly, and could hardly believe he was also at the Mid Integration Stage.

The Black Tortoise Shell guarded in front of Elder Bai Li Ting, while Elder Wu Shui hid in the White Bone Flying Boat, using the boat’s hull to block.

The little flood dragons were agile and versatile. They hit the Black Tortoise Shell, scattered into droplets, climbed along the shell’s surface, and then reformed into little flood dragons, besieging Bai Li Ting.

Elder Wu Shui took out the Ten Thousand Soul Banner, numerous lost souls wailed, controlling the boat’s cannons to bombard the little flood dragons.

The White Bone Flying Boat drifted and bobbed on the sea like a real ship, as well as crashing into rocks, shattering to pieces.

The little flood dragons, after being dispersed, condensed again as if they had endless life. Whatever magic skill had been imbued in these little flood dragons, they could use their bodies as cages, imprisoning souls within.

Even with ten thousand souls in Elder Wu Shui’s Ten Thousand Soul Banner, it couldn’t withstand such depletion.

Elder Wu Shui’s cultivation techniques were also related to water, which was why he knew how fierce Dai Bufan under such conditions was, and that he must be contained!

"Here, I set the rule: ’Rain shall not fall in Kaihuang City’."

Instantly, Kaihuang City turned into clear skies, and the little flood dragons made of rainwater also disappeared one by one.

A battle in the Body Integration Realm relies on setting up mutual restrictions with each rule established.

But Dai Bufan, faced with the rule set by Elder Wu Shui to disperse the clouds and rain, showed no intention of countering with his own rule.

He took out a red banner emblazoned with auspicious clouds; the moment the Five-colored Auspicious Cloud Banner was unfurled, countless intricate and beautiful characters flew from the banner, branding the void, layering one Array Method upon another.

The Array Method had nine layers, named the Nine-layered Pagoda Formation. Once the Pagoda Formation was activated, the two Elders instantly bent over, unable to stand straight.

"Xuanwu Manifestation!" Elder Bai Li Ting fused his spear with the Black Tortoise Shell, summoning the corpse of Xuan Wu, intending to break through the Great Formation with the weight of Xuan Wu.

No matter their sky-high abilities or methods to recover from injuries, they were of no use.

The two of them theoretically were on par with a Mid Integration Stage cultivator, but that was for an ordinary Mid Integration Stage cultivator.

If they encountered a cultivator like Dai Bufan of the Integration Realm, they’d end up no better than these two Elders.

Lou Nan, Vice Sect Hierarch of the Ruthless Sect, Early Tribulation Stage.

Two Semi-Immortals!

Although Lu Yang didn’t know how to resolve the Forgetfulness Poison, he knew there was someone who definitely could.

For instance, the Chasing Moon True Person who possessed the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo.

Just one face-to-face encounter, and Lou Nan had already fallen prey to Chasing Moon True Person’s move, totally unaware of it himself.

If this palm strike were to land, the entire Kaihuang City would be reduced to nothing!

Facing this terrifying attack, Vast Sea Daoist Lord, calm and composed, extended a finger swathed in the Mystic Yellow two energies, and poked towards the sky, dwarfed by the two giant black palms, this finger seemed too small to be seen.

But the moment the finger collided with the giant hand, it met an obstruction like the world’s barrier, unable to be pressed down any further.

Lou Nan gritted his teeth and sweated profusely, having exerted his full strength, yet compared to Vast Sea Daoist Lord, who seemed as calm as a breeze, this palm strike didn’t seem terrifying at all.

Putting aside Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s Semi-Immortal status, he was also a great power at the Pass Tribulation Peak, Lou Nan was merely at the Early Tribulation Stage, how could he possibly contend against him?

The Moonlight Power condensed into snowflakes and scattered over the human realm, bringing an extreme coldness, falling on the huge black palms. Crash—

The main source of income for the Seek Dao Sect is Refining Pills, but even so, the Sect could not mass-produce Elixirs for Integration Period Cultivators to use; they were all refined by the Seventh Elder and a few of his disciples.

Now, thankfully, making the Oblivion Pill doesn’t even require the use of a Pill Furnace, just feeding the medicine and drawing blood—quite convenient.

Depending on the dilution degree of the blood, it can be used by anyone ranging from Body Integration Great Powers to ordinary people.

At that moment, no matter how unpalatable the Buddha Country gruel might be, Lu Yang was hoping that the Fairy would keep it authentic.

May the Worldly Venerable bless... oh no, I mean may Eldest Senior Sister bless me.

Sky Gate Mountain had a kitchen used by Fairy Eternity during Ancient Times, and Eldest Senior Sister had kindly stocked it with plenty of ingredients.

She was always fair in her actions, not favoring anyone. Since she had made gruel for Yun Mengmeng, she couldn’t neglect the Second-in-command.

Lu Yang shivered, Why do I have a share too?

Lu Yang was inwardly torn and didn’t dare to eat right away, stealthily glancing at Yun Mengmeng beside him.

Yun Mengmeng ate a spoonful of the gruel with a smile, making satisfied noises and continuing to eat spoonful after spoonful.

Lu Yang was utterly astonished; could it be that Fairy Eternity outperformed herself this time, and it was actually delicious?

He finally made up his mind, ate a spoonful of the gruel, and immediately felt sour, sweet, bitter, spicy, and salty flavors overwhelm him, his head becoming dizzy.

With a bang, Lu Yang’s head hit the table. He saw Yun Mengmeng, who looked as if she was drunk, stand up unsteadily, giggling and pointing at Lu Yang.

"Eh, why are there three Second-in-commands?"

Sister Mengmeng, you were poisoned, why didn’t you say so earlier? If I had known, I wouldn’t have eaten it...

After an unknown amount of time, Lu Yang woke up from his deep slumber, his head foggy and aching fiercely: "What just happened?"

Fairy Eternity kindly looked after the Dynasty’s senior official: "Little Yang, you’re too tired from your trip to Buddha Country; you fell asleep halfway through your meal."

"Oh, then I’ll continue eating..."

"What just happened?"

"Little Yang, you’re too tired from your trip to Buddha Country; you fell asleep halfway through your meal."

That’s not right, he brought Tang Chuanwu back, so why was there still reincarnation?

Once he realized this, Lu Yang’s mind gradually woke up, and he suddenly lifted his head, his eyes full of confusion.

What happened just now, how had he fallen asleep, and why couldn’t he remember anything?

Why had it gotten dark?

And why was there a warm sensation in his stomach, had he made another breakthrough?

The diligent Fairy Eternity had already cleaned up the dishes and wiped the table, everything was just as it had been before Lu Yang started eating, quietly waiting for Lu Yang to wake up.

Every time Little Yang woke up, he would take a bite and then fall back asleep—this cycle repeated many times. After finishing a bowl of porridge, Little Yang finally slept soundly.

Even fighting off sleepiness to eat his own porridge proved just how delicious his cooking was.

"You have experienced too many cycles of reincarnation in Buddha Country, and while your physical body hasn’t been affected much, your spirit has taken a great toll. Look, you fell asleep just now."

"Is that so?" Lu Yang felt he wasn’t as tired as Fairy Eternity described.

"Where’s Sister Mengmeng?" Lu Yang faintly remembered her being here.

"Oh, she danced away."

Lu Yang showed a puzzled expression, vaguely grasping a clue, but he had just woken up and wasn’t very clear-headed, his mind working slowly.

"By the way, Fairy, do you know any body refining techniques?" When Lu Yang fought with the Ruthless Sect Elder, he realized that even though his physique was far superior to his peers, he was still vastly outmatched when facing an Integration Period Cultivator.

It would be best to cover this weakness.

"What’s so hard about refining the body? The simplest way is to get struck by lightning. It so happens we know people here; Little Yang, you can choose any kind of Thunder Tribulation you want."

"...Is there another way?" Lu Yang thought that cultivation should be progressive, there was no need to be so aggressive.

"Immortal Fairy has a unique body refining technique that has never been taught to outsiders."

Before obtaining the Eternity Dao Fruit, Fairy Eternity did not rely on self-detonation to fight her enemies but on her unique body refining technique to compete with the great ancient geniuses, enjoying unrivaled glory.

"What is it?"

"The Pill Furnace body refining method—throwing you into a pill furnace, repeatedly roasting you with True Fire, and then adding various medicinal herbs into the furnace, allowing you to absorb the medicinal properties of these herbs amid the flames. Doing this for forty-nine days straight, you’ll see initial results. If you think that’s not intense enough, you could burn for a hundred days."

"...Is there another method?" Lu Yang felt like asking Fairy Eternity for cultivation methods might not have been a wise decision.

Lu Yang rarely asked Fairy Eternity for advice, and she was brimming with confidence and eagerness.

"Ah, don’t be so picky, the body refining techniques of Immortal Fairy aren’t something just anyone is qualified to enjoy. You should be secretly delighted."

Fairy Eternity, without further discussion, took possession of Lu Yang and controlled his body to walk into the Fairy’s kitchen.

In the kitchen stood a three-legged pill furnace, its walls carved with nine dragons, four phoenixes, and other ancient beasts, clearly invaluable.

"Why is there a pill furnace here?!"

"What do you mean? Isn’t it very normal to cook with a pill furnace?" Fairy Eternity said matter-of-factly, feeling that Little Yang was too naive.

She controlled Lu Yang’s body to lift the furnace lid and climb inside.

Fairy Eternity snapped her fingers, and a raging fire blazed beneath the pill furnace, the unique Immortal Fairy Fire belonging to the Fairy.

The Laurel Fairy Palace used the Immortal Fairy Fire, a relic from Ancient Times, for refining pills, refining tools, and heating hot springs—a shared treasure among all the elders and disciples of the Fairy Palace. Yet, Lu Yang had the privilege of enjoying the Immortal Fire alone, a luxury only afforded to high-ranking officials of the Great Bean Dynasty!

With a mere thought from Fairy Eternity, the ingredients—or rather, medicinal herbs—near the kitchen wall began to float, orderly flying into the pill furnace.

Immortal Fairy Eternity was indeed a master at cooking; as the herbs entered the Pill Furnace and were scorched by the Immortal Fire, they instantly vaporized and then condensed into a few drops of Spiritual Liquid.

These few drops of Spiritual Liquid represented the most essential part of the herb, with all impurities already removed - a pill refining technique only top-tier Pill Grandmasters could employ.

More and more herbs flew into the Pill Furnace, turning into boiling Spiritual Liquid, merging with each other, some adhering to the furnace walls, some sinking to the bottom.

"Done, all that’s left is to cook."

Immortal Fairy Eternity borrowed and returned in kind, restoring control of the body back to Lu Yang.

Previously seized by possession, Lu Yang had not yet felt it; now, as he regained his physical body, he immediately sensed the horrifying high temperature of the Pill Furnace. Some kind of restriction had been placed on the furnace, preventing flight, leaving Lu Yang hopping back and forth with his burning feet.

And there were drops of boiling Spiritual Liquid spilling onto his body, causing a piercing pain.

"Ah—"

Lu Yang’s screams could be heard coming from the Pill Furnace; the pain caused him to crash against the furnace walls, but the Pill Furnace was as heavy as a mountain, clearly not something Lu Yang could move.

God knows how long it had been, maybe a quarter of an hour, perhaps a day; Lu Yang was scorched until he completely lost the ability to perceive time.

...

"Junior Brother, your idea is indeed feasible." After getting confirmation from the Seventh Elder, Yun Zhi sent the three members of the Ruthless Sect to Captive Peak to gradually bleed out. Returning to Sky Gate Mountain and hearing the screams coming from the Fairy Kitchen, she hurriedly went to investigate.

Upon entering the kitchen and seeing the burning Pill Furnace, Yun Zhi instantly understood what her Junior Brother was doing.

This must be the Fairy’s method.

Yun Zhi opened the furnace door and pulled Lu Yang out.

Lu Yang’s clothes had already turned to ash, and he himself was scorched black, looking like charred wood; only when he spoke could one discern where his mouth was by his teeth.

"Eldest Senior Sister..." Upon seeing his Eldest Senior Sister, Lu Yang looked as if he had seen his savior.

Then Lu Yang heard the Eldest Senior Sister chastise the Immortal Fairy Eternity, who was enjoying the show, "Fairy, how can one take shortcuts in Body Refinement? Merely placing oneself in the Pill Furnace to cook, what if it leaves behind hidden dangers for the future?"

"To refine the body, one must train under heavy loads, endure to strengthen the sinews and bones, train until one cannot get up, wring out every bit of strength from the body, and yet still continue to cultivate. Only then can the physical limits be broken, and this is the proper technique of Body Refining."

The charred Lu Yang’s complexion instantly turned pale as memories long suppressed surged in his heart.

In the year when he had just entered the Sect, the Eldest Senior Sister, to lay a solid foundation for him, endured day and night refining his body, only letting him go when he reached Foundation Establishment.

That time was so painful it made him feel worse than death, and the mere thought made him shiver.

The Eldest Senior Sister’s Body Refining technique was by no means lighter than the Fairy’s.

About matters concerning Lu Yang, Immortal Fairy Eternity would not show weakness, "This is this Immortal’s Body Refining Technique, how could there be any flaws? Look, isn’t this Immortal just fine?"

Yun Zhi spoke earnestly, "Body Refinement should follow the proper path. Looking for shortcuts could harm Junior Brother."

"My Body Refining method has no issues."

"The orthodox Body Refining technique is the Righteous Path."

"Little Yang, whose advice will you take?"

"Junior Brother, whose advice will you take?"

Immortal Fairy Eternity and Yun Zhi both looked down at Lu Yang, who was sprawled on the ground, still unable to recover his breath.

Lu Yang looked up, his eyes glistening with tears, his face a picture of utter despair.

Can I choose neither?

"Well, I think I don’t really need to pursue the Art of Body Refining too much; I’m quite content with how I am now," Lu Yang whispered, shivering like a cold-stricken quail, unable to look directly into the eyes of his Eldest Senior Sister and Fairy.

It wasn’t a matter of not wanting to offend either of them, but rather that choosing either option would likely cost him his life.

However, it was clear that neither Fairy Eternity nor Yun Zhi had any intention of letting him off the hook.

"How can that be acceptable? The Art of Body Refining is extremely important for cultivators. Look at this Immortal’s own body—oh, I do not presently have a physical form, but when I did, why do you think I was able to dominate the ancient times?

It’s because this Immortal’s cultivation had no weaknesses, whether it was Divine Abilities, magic skills, or physical tempering, I had everything," Fairy Eternity spoke from her own experience.

Fairy Eternity made her case.

"The Fairy elder speaks sensible words," Yun Zhi nodded in agreement.

Lu Yang felt a tingling in his scalp, realizing that he had no way to bypass this challenge and would need to find another method.

"The Body Refining Technique that the Fairy and Eldest Senior Sister possess must certainly be among the top in the world. What I mean is, is there a way to combine these two techniques?"

"For instance, Eldest Senior Sister’s orthodox Body Refinement practices involve toughening the sinews and bones, breaking through the physical limits, whereas Fairy, you refine the body in a pill furnace to help me absorb the essence of medicinal herbs."

"We could have me absorb the essence of medicinal herbs through taking a medicinal bath, using the essence to break through my body’s limits, and supplement that with appropriate exercise to improve absorption efficiency."

Lu Yang remembered that when his Eldest Senior Sister first taught him cultivation, it involved training by day and soaking in a medicinal bath by night.

Combining the two methods, there would be no need for toughening sinews and bones, no pill furnace for body refining—just soaking in a medicinal bath would suffice!

Fairy Eternity gave a soft exclamation of surprise, her eyes brightening: "Combining the two methods? That’s an approach I hadn’t considered; it could be worth a try."

Eldest Senior Sister appeared thoughtful, persuaded by Lu Yang’s proposal: "To take the best of both worlds, it does sound like an effective plan."

A beautiful day began.

Lu Yang woke up from his bed and went to the back of Sky Gate Mountain, namely Great Snow Mountain, and with a heave, he carried it and started running laps around Sky Gate Mountain, quickly becoming so exhausted that he was gasping for breath.

Chasing Moon True Person, who lived on Great Snow Mountain, accompanied Lu Yang’s running, jostling up and down with the rhythm.

After finishing his laps, Lu Yang returned Great Snow Mountain to its original location and continued with his squats while carrying it.

"One, two, three... one thousand."

Lu Yang silently counted, completing a standard one thousand weighted squats. His warm-up was done.

He then tore open a Teleportation Talisman and with a flash before his eyes, the scenery changed; he found himself before the pitch-black waters of a sea where visibility was next to none.

This was the deepest part of the East Sea, where the water pressure was terrifyingly high, quickly crushing ordinary magic artifacts to thin sheets of metal, which was why a Water-Repelling Pearl was essential when coming to the East Sea.

But Lu Yang did not bring a Water-Repelling Pearl.

Standing there, he felt as though he was bound with thousands of his own weight, encountering immense resistance with every movement and requiring all his muscular strength to act, truly a struggle.

"Little Yang, keep it up; this Immortal believes in you," cheered Fairy Eternity, moving effortlessly and unaffected in that place, waving her flag enthusiastically in support of Lu Yang.

Lu Yang, fully immersed in his cultivation, assumed his stance and executed the Lu Family Arhat Fist, each move slow as if in a replay, extremely slow-motion.

After one set of Arhat Fist, Lu Yang was so tired he was panting, arms trembling, without the strength to even stand on the seabed; his body relaxed and he began to drift upwards.

Lu Yang floated from the depths of the East Sea all the way to the surface, the changing pressures during this journey causing him immense discomfort as if all his organs were crushed together, indistinguishable from one another.

He floated on the sea surface, drifting with the waves, and as the sea eagles circled above him, he shakily took out a Teleportation Talisman from his bosom and transported himself back to Sky Gate Mountain.

Puppets had long been waiting silently for Lu Yang’s return at Sky Gate Mountain.

Upon seeing Lu Yang teleported back, a Puppet stuffed a top-quality Great Recovery Pill into Lu Yang’s mouth, allowing him to regain his strength.

To assist in Lu Yang’s Body Refining, Eldest Senior Sister had cleared a place on Sky Gate Mountain and set up a Gravity Array. Once he had recovered his strength, Lu Yang entered the Array and felt his limbs as heavy as if they were filled with lead, unable to lift them.

In such a condition, he needed to wield the Green Peak Sword to hone his Swordsmanship.

Whenever Lu Yang could no longer swing his sword, a Puppet would appear and feed him Great Recovery Pills.

After an unknown number of repetitions, eventually, Lu Yang took Great Recovery Pills without any effect, powerless, he closed his eyes and collapsed to the ground with a thud.

Lu Yang’s eyelids drooped, simply too tired to open his eyes.

Seeing this, the Puppet carried on with the procedure and carried Lu Yang to the Fairy’s kitchen.

By this time, Immortal Fairy had already finished preparations, with the Immortal Fire burning vigorously, its intense heat felt even from a distance.

The Puppet opened the furnace door, and a wave of hot air rushed out.

Hoisting Lu Yang by his legs, the Puppet stuffed him inside, and throughout the process, Lu Yang didn’t even have the energy to struggle or resist.

Various aged herbal medicines, under Immortal Fairy’s control, flew into the Pill Furnace and refined into Spiritual Liquid, dripping onto Lu Yang’s body.

"All set, the rest depends on how well Little Yang absorbs it," said Immortal Fairy gleefully, clapping her hands, her task for the day successfully completed, and now it was just a matter of waiting for Little Yang to "come out of the pot."

"In the morning, he trains his body to break through its limits, and in the afternoon, he is put into the Pill Furnace to absorb the medicinal properties. He not only absorbs the properties but also replenishes what his body lacks."

"Little Yang is smart indeed to think of combining my method with Miss Yun’s. Why didn’t I think of this before?"

On the basis of Lu Yang’s proposed method, Immortal Fairy had made improvements, allowing her and Yun Zhi’s methods to be more effectively combined, and the results were significant.

"It seems Little Yang is quite adapted to this method now. He used to cry out when entering the furnace, but now he doesn’t make a sound."

Lu Yang’s face was against the floor, lying at the bottom of the Pill Furnace, closest to the Immortal Fire.

He felt an excruciating pain, and he could even smell the scent of charred flesh.

Lu Yang had the intention to cry out in pain, but he was too exhausted to even summon the energy to scream, leaving him to the mercy of the furnace’s roasting.

"Fairy, this isn’t the combination method that I wanted..."

After a while, seeing that Lu Yang was roasted enough, the Puppet opened the furnace door and pulled him out.

Unlike the previous time when the process was interrupted halfway by Yun Zhi, this time, after an afternoon of roasting, Lu Yang’s body underwent a transformation from charred to the growth of new skin, emerging clean and white, exuding a medicinal fragrance.

The Puppet carried Lu Yang back to the Abode, allowing him to rest for a good night.

In his sleep, nightmares struck, and Heavenly Venerate Tofu reappeared, cheering on Lu Yang, hoping he would persevere.

...

A beautiful day began.

Lu Yang woke up from the bed, his eyes devoid of any brightness.

Lu Yang staggered like a walking corpse, struggling on the verge of life and death.

A hundred and ten days had passed, his virtues had reached consummation, and he had achieved some success in body refinement, temporarily escaping from the bitter sea.

The moment he realized that the cultivation ended, Lu Yang looked bewildered and fell asleep instantly, sleeping continuously for three days.

Upon awakening, he saw Fairy Eternity.

"Congratulations, congratulations," Fairy Eternity clapped squawkily.

At that moment, Lu Yang’s body was enshrouded in a hazy golden light, impervious to ordinary attacks. This Protective Golden Light was a symbol of ultimate body refinement.

No candles were lit in the abode; it was pitch-black inside. With the Protective Golden Light, Lu Yang was as conspicuous as a little golden statue. During the three days of Lu Yang’s sleep, he had been shining brightly continuously.

The Protective Golden Light was part of Lu Yang, and even without being taught, he could manage it freely. The first thing he did upon waking was to quickly retract the light—it was too dazzling.

Reflecting on the days of the past hundred days, Lu Yang felt extraordinarily fortunate. novelbuddy.cσ๓

"It’s good I brought back Tang Chuanwu. If he had performed Time Retrospection again, who knows what might have happened."

Though these days didn’t feel different from having experienced Time Retrospection.

Lu Yang lay in bed, his mind blank, feeling incredibly happy not having to endure weight training or being stuffed into an alchemy furnace.

He clasped and then loosened his hand, feeling the vigorous power contained within his body, a stark contrast to the past—so much so that if he could block out the incessant noise from Fairy Eternity, he could even hear the sound of his blood flowing.

"It wasn’t torment for nothing."

Despite the enormous gains, Lu Yang was not keen on experiencing the torment of body refinement by Fairy Eternity and Eldest Senior Sister again.

It was hardly a life for anyone.

"Second-in-command, there is someone with the last name Ao at the gate of the sect looking for you," Yun Mengmeng knocked on Lu Yang’s abode door and shouted, relaying the message from the discipled guarding the sect’s entrance.

"Someone with the surname Ao?" Lu Yang stepped out of the abode, somewhat puzzled.

Wasn’t that Ao Ling? What did she want with him?

Lu Yang exited the sect and saw three unfamiliar women.

"Senior Brother Lu, don’t you recognize us?" one of the women teased.

"It’s Junior Sister...Senior Ao Ling, ah," Lu Yang suddenly realized; these three were clearly Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi in disguise.

As for the third person, judging by her stature, it must be Jin Caiwei.

The relationship between Ao Ling’s trio and Lu Yang was confidential; even within the Seek Dao Sect, only a very few knew about it. To avoid trouble, they had come to see Lu Yang in disguise.

"Please, come inside quickly." Lu Yang hastily invited the three women in.

They were three Semi-Immortals, and both ethically and logically, he couldn’t let them stay outside.

The three women followed Lu Yang into the Seek Dao Sect and headed towards Sky Gate Mountain, where they removed their disguises to reveal their stunningly beautiful true faces.

"What brings you here?" Lu Yang smiled, pouring tea and water for the three women.

"Enlightenment Tea?" Jin Caiwei displayed a look of astonishment; she hadn’t tasted such a vintage of Enlightenment Tea in a long time.

"It’s Wei who wanted to see you," Ao Ling smiled, as she and Jiang Lianyi were just passing by.

Jin Caiwei sat in the Emperor’s Chair, her feet not touching the ground, holding her teacup and feeling embarrassed under Lu Yang’s stare.

Jin Caiwei spoke softly with her head lowered, "I was wondering, the Oblivion Pill that has recently appeared on the market, does it have anything to do with you, Young Sect Master?"

Since purchasing candles to corner the market, the already impoverished Qiongqi Clan had become even poorer.

Jin Caiwei had accidentally learned that the Oblivion Pill, which had recently become very popular in Great Xia, originated from the Seek Dao Sect, and felt it might be related to Lu Yang, the Young Sect Master, hence she shamelessly came to seek cooperation.

In the agonizing past three months for Lu Yang, the Oblivion Pill experiment had succeeded, received approval from the Dynasty for sales within the boundaries of Great Xia, and was widely praised; describing it as earning a fortune daily would seem an understatement.

"Somewhat related, but all I did was provide a small idea," Lu Yang humbly said, having roughly guessed the purpose of this Emperor of Vast Wealth of the North Pole visiting him.

Upon hearing that it indeed had something to do with Lu Yang, Jin Caiwei’s eyes lit up, "Then, Young Sect Master, could you think of a way to let our Qiongqi Clan become the agent for selling elixirs in the Demon Territory?"

If they could become the agents in the Demon Territory, their Qiongqi Clan would certainly not be so poor anymore.

"I see..." Jin Caiwei, upon being refused by Lu Yang, was quite disheartened.

"However, Senior Jin, if you wish to make money, it’s not necessarily the only way through agency."

"What is it?"

"Since Senior’s Plane Dao Fruit Outline can compress three-dimensional objects into two dimensions, and turn two-dimensional objects into three-dimensional ones, have you ever tried, compressing what you see into two dimensions?"

Lu Yang, smiling, stood up and pointed towards the scenery of Seek Dao Sect, "Painters, upon seeing beautiful sceneries, will paint them as keepsakes. Could Senior mimic this act by compressing this beautiful scenery into two dimensions and imprinting it?"

Jin Caiwei seemed to understand, yet not quite, and she took out a piece of paper, activated the Plane Dao Fruit Outline, and imprinted the scenery of Seek Dao Sect onto the paper.

"Like this?"

She activated the Plane Dao Fruit Outline, and the Recording Orb projected a beam of light in which two lifelike figures were fighting.

"Is this my battle with Zhu Tian?" Jiang Lianyi saw herself in the Recording Orb.

Jiang Lianyi’s fight with Zhu Tian during the founding ceremony of the Demon Nation had been recorded by many and widely circulated; Lu Yang had also bought a copy of the Recording Orb as a souvenir.

"Senior could apply the ability of the Plane Dao Fruit Outline on the Recording Orb, making all the scenes played by the Recording Orbs three-dimensional. It should fetch a good price."

Jin Caiwei still couldn’t believe that her Dao Fruit Outline could actually make money, but seeing the Young Sect Master looking so confident, it seemed there might really be a viable plan.

in order to convince Jin Caiwei, Lu Yang discussed successful case studies with her.

Immortal, is your ranking system reliable?

In an unknown land, towering palaces pierced the clouds, resembling the elusive Fairy Palace of legends.

Within the Fairy Palace, murals depicted bizarre events, massive giants riding divine oxen to plow the earth, saints splashing ink to paint among the stars, divine beings descending to dispel demons and bring peace to the world... Thirty thousand years had passed, yet the murals remained as vivid as if freshly painted, as if the painter had just left moments ago.

If any denizens of Great Qian were here, they would easily recognize these events as the legends passed down orally, and the protagonists of these legends were none other than the Heavenly God Immortals, renowned for their great virtues under the Great Qian Dynasty.

Among the murals, the most conspicuous depicted the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord standing above the ninth heaven, supporting the sun with one hand, the moon with the other, worshipped by the Heavenly God Immortals.

"Wuhu, New Year is coming."

For cultivators with extended lifespans, it is customary to celebrate once every ten years, and Seek Dao Sect was no exception.

Not just in Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space, but the entire Seek Dao Sect was filled with joyous vibes, with big red decorations visible everywhere. "Is the Second-in-command so childish? I stopped doing that when I was sixteen."

"This mortal really is a bit odd," the Nian Beast said playfully. Being naturally curious and lively Demon Beasts, they wouldn’t otherwise mix in with the crowds and play every year.

With a roar, the Nian Beast lunged at Lu Yang, who swung his arm in a full circle and smashed it down. Since his physical body had improved, he found close combat quite amusing.

"I’m not afraid of you!"

The two wrestled together, with the Nian Beast overpowering Lu Yang and roaring in his face, dousing him with saliva.

"Three Flavored True Fire, ptui!"

Lu Yang had initially learned the Three Flavored True Fire to release it through his mouth and catch his enemy off guard, but he had never expected to use it on a Nian Beast.

The Nian Beast was singed by the Three Flavored True Fire, its mane shriveled and curled into tiny black dots. Seeing this, Lu Yang flipped over and gained the upper hand.

The fierce battle between man and beast was unpredictable, and the complex politics involved were truly astonishing.

That is, if you could see the Nian Beast.

"Second-in-command, why did you suddenly start rolling?" Yun Mengmeng asked in confusion. She heard that New Year’s Money also serves as Money to Suppress Evil Spirits, so could it be that Second-in-command didn’t get enough and got cursed?

"I’m fighting a Nian Beast; you can’t see it," Lu Yang replied, before being pinned down by the Nian Beast again.

"You’re supposed to be the legendary Nian Beast; can’t you use some other attack methods!" Lu Yang yelled angrily, feeling as primitive as a caveman.

"Lose the battle, not the war. You use a different method, and then I’ll use another!"

"Ptui!"

"Ptui!"

Neither wanted to admit being outmatched in close combat, resolutely refusing to use any other methods, simply competing in physical strength, power, and melee skills.

Seeing Lu Yang like this, Yun Mengmeng actually believed he wasn’t just fantasizing; he really was fighting an invisible enemy.

She tried to touch the Nian Beast by feeling, but her hand passed right through it, touching nothing.

Yun Mengmeng didn’t know that the Nian Beast, cultivated from the Time Dao Fruit, was inherently related to time, having completed a life transition to an entirely different level of existence.

"Second-in-command, do you need my help?"

"No need, I refuse to believe I can’t beat it!" Lu Yang’s veins bulged as he was determined to overpower the Nian Beast.

Immortal Fairy was hopping up and down in the Spiritual Space, providing Lu Yang with spiritual support, as fighting the Nian Beast had become a traditional New Year’s custom.

As Lu Yang and the Nian Beast were locked in a stalemate, suddenly, a line of fiery clouds appeared on the horizon, rapidly approaching the direction of the Seek Dao Sect.

As the fiery clouds came closer, Lu Yang realized that these were not clouds at all, but a flock of Nian Beasts!

The leader of the Nian Beasts was as large as a small hill, exuding a terrifying pressure as the Clan Leader of the Nian Beasts.

Facing the sight of the younger Nian Beast here, the Clan Leader’s expression drastically changed: "Chujie, what are you doing? Didn’t I tell you never to come to the Seek Dao Sect, our clan’s forbidden zone, because of the terrifying major demon!"

"Beware the major demon might suddenly appear and capture you!"

Seeing the Clan Leader leading the clan members, the younger Nian Beast no longer dared to frolic with Lu Yang, pushing him away reluctantly, "Clan Leader, I’m not a child anymore. Don’t think I don’t know, all this major demon stuff is a hoax—I’ve been here so long and haven’t seen any major demon!"

"Foolish!" the Nian Beast Clan Leader roared in anger. "I nearly didn’t escape when I encountered the major demon. Do you think you’d still be jumping around if you had seen her?"

The Nian Beast Clan Leader then bit the neck of the younger Nian Beast and flung it onto his back.

For some reason, though the Clan Leader didn’t specify, Lu Yang instinctively felt that the "major demon" he mentioned was the Eldest Senior Sister.

It was infuriating that he dared to slander the Eldest Senior Sister right in front of him.

Eldest Senior Sister was such a good person, teaching her own cultivation methods, and even rushing to help when facing danger. How could such a person be a major demon?

"Hm, you can see us?"

Only then did the Clan Leader of the Nian Beast notice Lu Yang’s presence. It lay on the ground, its huge brown pupils reflecting Lu Yang’s tiny figure.

"Interesting boy, could it be that you have been blessed by an Immortal?" The Clan Leader, having seen much, realized that indeed there were such mortals who could sense their presence—each one undoubtedly lucky, cherished by the Immortals.

"Is that a wooden plaque from our lord that you are wearing around your neck?" The Clan Leader felt a familiar power emanating from Lu Yang’s chest.

"Are you referring to this? It was given to me by someone from the Five Elements Sect." Lu Yang took out a wooden plaque, which was a part from the Firmament Tree.

"Our lord’s Immortal Corpse..." The Clan Leader looked at the wooden plaque, lost in thought.

It had learned from the previous Clan Leader where the Immortal Corpse of their lord was buried.

"Wait a moment, let me call someone over." Seeing that the Clan Leader had never seen the Time Immortal but felt something for a wooden plaque, Lu Yang directly brought over a confused Li Haoran.

"Look at him, do you feel anything familiar?"

The Clan Leader frowned, unsure why Lu Yang had brought this person over.

"What feeling could I possibly have? This person can’t even see us."

Lu Yang frowned. The Clan Leader felt absolutely nothing towards Li Haoran?

"Ah well, since you can see us and possess our lord’s wooden plaque, it seems it’s also fate. It’s rare for creatures to detect our presence, so let us take you for a ride!"

The Clan Leader stopped thinking about the Time Immortal. It wasn’t in their joyous Tnature as beings of the Nian species. Due to being on a different plane of existence, they couldn’t communicate with other beings. Meeting someone like Lu Yang, a fortunate soul, naturally meant they should treat him well.

"This..."

"Come now, this is a chance many people would envy."

Without allowing Lu Yang any objections, the Clan Leader bit Lu Yang’s collar and, in the same manner as it handled a little Nian Beast, tossed him onto its back.

The Nian Beast species, having basically never encountered a creature that could talk to them, were all very excited, crowding around and chattering endlessly.

"Brother, which Immortal did you encounter?"

"In what way did the Immortal take notice of you?"

"Did you see us last year?"

"How did you end up fighting with New Year’s Day, and who won?"

"Enough, enough, shut up, I’m going to start flying now!" the Clan Leader shouted, its form turning ethereal.

Lu Yang entered a mysterious state, facing an endless stream of water blowing against him, making it impossible for him to open his eyes.

He struggled to open one eye and realized he was in the midst of the stream of time, where the experiences of his past appeared like slides on either side—from joining the Seek Dao Sect, slaying the Tiger Demon during his Foundation Establishment Stage, infiltrating the Eternity Sect, reviving the Immortal Fairy, founding the Heavenly Court... up until tonight’s New Year’s Eve.

Just when Lu Yang thought it was going to end, more images continued to appear on both sides!

The images were extremely blurry, but Lu Yang could only make out one.

In the image, the world of the box slowly unfolded, revealing a boundless, shimmering starry sky.

Boom!

The Clan Leader carried Lu Yang as they burst out of the time stream, the surrounding images collapsing.
